<Author>exploremore1
<Content>Great! This was a great hotel. I used booking.com, they had really good rates. The price was very reasonable. The front desk staff were extremely helpful and patient about every question and request. They give you free lemonade, beer, and water in the minibar which is cool. The room was beautiful and the view was excellent. The shower was great, there were 6 different water spouts. The only problem is the water comes out on the floor, but this was a minor problem. The glass wall for the bathroom was an interesting, pretty touch. The room was very nice, it was great to wake up and go to sleep to that view of the city. You can take the metro to the hotel very easily, and you can take the tram to many different places. Just be careful, the area seems very safe and far apart from the main mix of things, but I had my purse stolen not too far from the hotel. There is a great mall right next door for shopping and also to grab food and snacks at the last minute. I loved this hotel; it's great for family or friends, and especially a romantic trip. I would stay here again definitely. They also give free robes and slippers, which they continually refresh! Also, they clean the room whenever you leave, even if it's in the afternoon (most rooms are only cleaned in the morning!).

<Author>Sorrentina06
<Content>Excellent Experience I stayed here for 3 nights recently with my boyfriend and we were both extremely impressed with the hotel and the services offered. We paid a little extra for the Wellness Package which proved to be excellent value for money. We had a room on the 18th Floor which provided spectacular views over the city. The robes, slippers, free mini bar (replenished free of charge every day), toiletries (including toothbrush and toothpaste, comb, nail file etc) were very much appreciated and the included breakfast was second to none (everything you could possibly want...and more).I took advantage of the included free massage (1 per day if you want it - 1 hour for 1 person or 2 half hour sessions for both) which did wonders for my back and my boyfriend tried out the hot tub/jacuzzi and sauna.We found the staff to be always professional, helpful and friendly.As for the location? No complaints there at all. The hotel is very close to the beach and line 4 on the Metro (5 mins walk) which has many of the must visit locations including Passeig de Gracia, Barceloneta etc. There is an impressive shopping centre 3 mins from the hotel which houses a huge supermarket (should you need extra drinks, food etc) as well as many other shops.All of the above contributed to a very pleasant stay. I would rate this hotel as a very good 4 star if not a 5 star (and it's a very close call). We wouldn't stay anywhere else if (which is very likely) were to return to Barcelona in the future and would certainly recommend it to all of our friends.

<Author>BrumTravelgirl
<Content>Beautiful view I chose the hotel based on reviews on trip advisor. I was a little sceptical of the location (being on the outskirts of the main tourist centre) but I was eventually persuaded one by the reviews and two by the competitive price.Turns out that its location was its biggest pull. We were given a room on the 17th floor, opened the blind which sheilds the floor to ceiling / wall to wall window to see the most amazing view of the city. It was even better at night.The room was very trendy too. There was an amazing shower with jets and what i can only refer to as a waterfall shower.Location wise, it was actually rather good. Attractions in Barcelona are pretty spread out so it's best to get to terms with the metro system. There is a metro stop literally minutes away and you can be in the centre within 15 minutes of leaving the hotel. If you are not so keen on using the metro there was a stop for the open top tourist bus right outside the hotel.

<Author>NPWParis
<Content>Great value, geat views This hotel, which we didn't know beforehand, turned out to be a great value choice for a weekend in Barcelona. The rate was 120 euros per night for two including full breakfast. This hotel is a new tower block at the seaward end of the Diagonal, a little too far from the centre to walk but with metro, tram and bus connections, and great views over the Mediterranean and the city. Rooms are cleverly designed to make the best use of space and the warm wooden panelling is remarkably lavish given the room rates. The design in the rest of the hotel is far more convincing than at La Florida up on Tibidabo, where I stayed for the previous two nights, and at half the price. The breakfast room is fairly spartan but the buffets are unusually generous and there's something for everyone: eggs, bacon and so on, but also grilled vegetables, Spanish specialities and a vast selection of pastries. A very good base for visiting the city.

<Author>TM_Trademark
<Content>Great hotel Stayed at this hotel for 3 nights. Views are fabulous. Hotel staff was helpful and polite. Enjoyed the complimentary minibar and the great bathroom shower. Bed was firm but comfortable. The blackout shades on the window and glass bathroom wall worked well. Even though the hotel isn't very close to the main tourist areas, we had no problem using the subway and tram to get around. <Author>liv83
<Content>Good for relaxing holiday On arrival we spoke to an unfriendly younger male staff member. He gave us a room on a 20+ floor. Upon arrival in the room we noticed it was a smoking room. Both of us are non-smokers and we had requested a non-smoking room. When we pointed this out, another staff member quickly gave us the only non-smoking room left, which had a sea view but no useable balcony.The room was very clean and welcoming to come home to at night. We liked the free minibar, although it would ve been better if you could choose the drinks in it beforehand. The bed was amazing and consisted of two rather large individual mattresses. We fell in the space between them once but that was our own fault. The window blinds are excellent. The ensuite bathroom gave the room a cold, modern look and was not entirely practical. We got it out of sight by putting down the blinds in between room and bathroom. The toilet offers virtually no privacy. It isnt even possible to close it properly and it has a see through door. Luckily there are plenty of toilets available on the lower floors.The shower was fantastic. It is built for taller people, but you can change the direction of the showerheads so that was not a problem. Amenities were good.Always keep the do not disturb sign on when you don't want the room to be made up yet, as the housekeeping staff are very quick to go in. I also found them to be the best housekeeping staff I've ever encountered. Very friendly. One lady went out of her way to find us two bathrobes and everyone was very courteous.What truly made our stay was the breakfast. It was excellent in every way. Staff was very professional. Variety was very good. Truly relaxing start of the day.The swimming pool are 'lounging areas' rather than meant for actual swimming. Lounging chairs were occupied pretty early every day. The swimming pool downstairs is too chilly, with everyone able to look at you when walking aroundin the hotel. The swimming pool on the 23rd floor offers a great view of the sea. However, only one person can swim in it at once so its at best used as an occasional refreshment. The area quickly got very very crowded on a sunny day, with people lounging very close to eachother without available chairs left.Location is rather far from city sights, but close to the beach and to the big shopping complex right next door. Not good location for experiencing nightlife unless you take a cab.Overall, we had a very relaxing stay, thoroughly enjoyed breakfast and would come back next time we visit Barcelona.  
<Date>Sep 4, 2008

<Author>iandi08
<Content>Loved it! We stayed here for a short city break and it was fantastic!Check in was easy and we were upgraded to a junior suite. Our room was a great size with free mini bar which was replenished every day with water, coke, lemonade and a bottle of lager. The room was very clean and we were provided with clean towels, robes and slippers daily. We didn't book for breakfast and it was expensive to add on. However, we found lovely cafes in the centre to have a lazy morning breakfast so didn't miss it.The pool at the top of the hotel is long and very narrow but perfect for a short dip after all that sight seeing. There is also a second pool on the third floor with a lounge and bar area.The hotel is situated a bit out of the city but the hop on hop off bus stops right outside which makes travelling very easy. There is also a metro stop very close by and the trains run quite late, again making it easy to get about. We work in London so are used to the tube system, perhaps others might not want to use this mode of transport late at night, although we felt perfectly safe. It was only a 20 minute journey on the metro so a taxi would be quicker. There are also regular buses if you can figure them out!The hotel is perfect for the beach, just a short walk away. The beach, although man made, is brilliant. A perfect contrast to the busy city.Next door to the hotel is a huge shopping centre with lots of shops, including a large supermarket in the basement. As part of the centre there is a selection of restaurants which are outside and in a pedestrian area. They are great for eating, drinking and watching the world go by. Nice alternative rather than going back into the centre. The food here was better than that in the hugely touristy areas.Every visitor to Barcelona must get on the hop on hop off bus tour - as city tours go, it's the best I've been on. There are 3 routes and you can chop and change as much as you want. They visit all the must see sights of Barcelona and it gives you an opportunity to rest your legs!Please don't be put off this hotel because of the location - it's really great!

<Author>yourterriblemuriel
<Content>A great stay we stayed at the Princess for just one night during a South of France holiday. It was definately worth the 2 hour drive, and we wished we could have stayed longer. <Author>Holmesey
<Content>A bit too far out... The hotel is not bad, clean and well maintained. Bedrooms are on the small side and as the beds are quite large it feels a little bit claustrophobic. Extras such as breakfast and laundry are expensive. The staff seemed not bothered most of the time and I often had to grab someones attention even though I was the only person standing at the counter! However, my biggest gripe is the distance from the centre of Barcelona. Despite previous comments I found the journey arduous. The Metro is quite close but it's still a 20 minute ride to Cataluyna station. It was sometimes hard to get taxis in the evening, particularly from 8 o'clock onwards and cost about 12 euro to get to the city. However Barcelona can be difficult to get a taxi from in the early hours and I spent over an hour trying to hail a cab one night wishing my hotel was more central.The princess is not a bad hotel and the beach around teh corner is great however I would highly recommend staying more central.

<Author>JulieStevenage_Herts
<Content>Great Hotel Just returned from our second trip to the Barcelona Princess and had a great time. Our room was on the 14th floor, overlooking the city from where we could see a number of the major sights of Barcelona. We loved the large bed, the mini bar, excellent shower / wet room and the bath robes. Although the hotel is out of the city, the hop on hop off bus stops just outside. Also the Metro is just around the corner, and taxis are in good supply. We ate breakfast at a cafe over the road, as in the hotel it would have cost us 16 euros, this was despite an internet offer for complimentary breakfast which wasn't available to us because I didn't book direct with the hotel. We also enjoyed drinks in the corner bar, particularly the Cava which was just great. I would highly recommend this hotel, but book direct!

<Content>Excellent, Fabulous Hotel All I can say is this was the perfect hotel to stay in. The Metro is literally 2 minutes away. Honestly I cannot find one thing that is bad to say about this hotel. The staff were really friendly. It was so easy to get around Barcelona and really nice to come back to a place that was peaceful. I read all the reviews before I left and was worried it was far away from the sights but that is so not true. Enjoy it was absolutely wonderful!!!

<Author>B0wz
<Content>Enjoyable Stay A 20 minute taxi drive from the airport this hotel is nicely situated on the outskirts of the city, near the brand new forum section of barcelona. The hotel is ideal for people looking for a comfortable stay away from the hussle of the city but close to the beach.The location for the beach in the summer is fantastic, only about a 5 minute walk. And although outside the city center a bus stop right outside the hotel means that this problem is solved within 10 minutes.We booked into the hotel late in the evening and were quickly allocated a room. The room was spacious without being too big. The minibar was well stocked with drinks and the bathroom was very impressive. We also had a balcony which overlooked the main road into the city, i had expected it to be noisey but the car traffic 15 floors below really was not noticable.The hotel features a pool which was my only complaint, the pool on the top floor was reasonably warm when the sun was on it but when the sun went over at about 4pm the pool quickly cooled down and really was a little too cold. Also the top floor pool section has limited seating and we found that all the seats were quickly taken by about 8am.The pool on the 3rd floor was even worse, i only ventured into it once and it was really unbearably cold (this was suprising because the outside temp was 28 - 35 Oc. This meant the pools in the hotel were a bit disappointing. The jacuzzi was pleasent and usually there was space to use it. Only on 2 occasions it was full. The sauna was the best part of the hotel in terms of ease of use, they have 2 seperate saunas and they were always empty meaning a nice relaxing 30 minutes was more or less guarenteed.The food in the hotel was pleasant, not too pricey and had reasonably big portions.The drinks at the bar at the front of the hotel were quite expensive but my god! 8 Euros for a jack daniels and i think he gave me the whole bottle!!Overall the hotel well worth 4 star, good bedrooms, good service near to the beach and a short bus ride to the city center.Would come back to this hotel again if i was looking for a relaxing hotel near the beach in Europes best city.

<Author>lots54
<Content>Highly recommended I have just returned from a short break staying at the Barcelona Princess Hotel. All in all, this was a fantastic hotel. I would recommend asking for a room as high up as possible (as long as you don't suffer from vertigo!) with the city view. You get views from the huge windows across the entire city. Free mini bar was useful and the bathroom and blackout blinds were great. Although the hotel is not in the centre of Barcelona, it was very easy to get round the city. There is a metro station (El Maresme Forum I) within 2 minutes walking distance from the hotel, and you can get into central Barcelona in about 10 minutes on the metro. I would highly recommend using the metro, as it is a very quick and cheap way to get around. The shopping centre is loacted next to the hotel. Within this you can find a huge supermarket, although the restaurants are all chain restaurants so I would recommend venturing further into the city to eat. Barcelenta has some good restaurants by the port, particulalry if you like fish.Some quick tips? If your going to use the public transport, purchase a T10 ticket at any of the metro or train terminals. This costs about 7 EUROS and lasts for 10 journeys on any of the public transport options. The open top bus tours are a good way of seeing the city and you can hop on and hop off. although be carful as these can be fairly busy.All in all a great hotel in a great part of the world.

<Author>theperks
<Content>Amazing Hotel We stayed at the Barcelona Princess around 18 months ago and have been very lazy about writing the review. This is no refection on the hotel, just me being lazy . . . . .The hotel is brilliant, couldn't fault it. Accepted it's not in the centre of the city but for me that's part of the appeal, it's very close (two minute walk tops) to a metro station and a tram stop to get in and out of town and being near apartment blocks you can get a feel for how the locals live in this great city.There's also a shopping centre nearby (again two minute walk) with bars, basic restaurants (Pizza Express) and a supermarket .The hotel is very modern with professional friendly staff, spotless rooms with the most amazing views of the city (as another member said, ask for a city view) and really cool features like electric blackout blinds and and insanely brilliant shower.Don't let the location put you off, this is what makes it more affordable as if this was in the centre it'd cost double to stay here, it is easy to get to the sights and we even walked it more than once.Going to Barcelona, stay here!

<Author>Tag_Beak
<Content>A Stylish Hotel Stayed here on 27-30 Dec and was well impressed. We were on 20th Floor with a City view. If you get the choice of sea/city view like us it has to be City. You could see the whole of Barcelona including many of the sights including Sagrada Familia. The rooms are really modern. There are electronic blinds covering the huge windows which look out over the city.If you dont like heights the glass elevator might worry you a bit but we loved it. Nice bar on the ground floor with decent prices. The free mini bar in the room is stocked each day with one estrella beer, coke, fanta and two waters. Breakfast was really good. Lots of choice, good food, nice dining room. The earlier you go the better as some things ran out after 10am.We took the metro everywhere. The Maresme Forum station is two mins walk from the hotel and its about 6/7 stops to the edge of the Barri Gotic. Get T10 tickets - 10 trips for about 7 EUR.Barcelona:-We did the camp nou tour. Well worth the money. Got the metro from hotel to Collblanc station. Then its about 10 min walk.Took the cable car to Montjuic Castle. The views are superb from up there.Eating and Drinking in barcelona can be hit and miss. Restaurants are generally quite small in the barri gotic area. We found them quite full and cramped. Dont go to TAPAS GAUDI which is on a street off Las Ramblas. This place wasn't full, probably because they serve awful luke warm tapas.

<Content>Excellent Hotel Stayed here in Sept 2007, Found the staff friendly  helpful. <Author>baah-humbug
<Content>Great showers, but grumpy uncaring staff and bad location. What a shame. This is a stunning building with great views and lovely showers. However, the staff are grumpy and there is a big problem with noise at night from a nearby club.When we stayed the metro branch that went near the hotel was closed for maintenance (which was told to us with an uncaring shrug from the reception staff) so we went by bus. Full of local colour but very slow, stopping every 25 metres or so. The area around is dead (except for the shopping arcade next door) and very unlike the rest of Barcelona which is buzzy and fun.I didn't feel like the staff cared who came and went, or whether we were enjoying ourselves or not. A very contemporary, minimalist interior. Which is great, except that it is really starting to show signs of wear and tear already. To sum up, this hotel lacks a feeling of care and attention (either to the guests or to the fabric of the hotel itself).In retrospect we would definitely have stayed nearer the centre of the city.

<Author>FrancesBedfordshire
<Content>We will not stay here again We stayed here for 5 nights on floor 21, rooms 17 18 (junior suite). Room 18 has a balcony but if you have young children, I would not recommend letting them outside on the balcony without an adult. There is a CD player in room 18. Room 17 has a bath with a shower. Room 18 has a shower with jets which, is really nice and relaxing to use but unfortunately, the water leaks out all over the bathroom floor and I don't mean drips, I mean a lot of water so you have to shower really quickly and then use 2 or 3 towels to soak up the water. We had a view of the sea from our rooms. The drinks in the fridge in your room are free. Water, coke, lemonade and cheap beer.On Friday night, my husband and I got woken by really loud music and some guy talking really loud on a microphone. This was around midnight. The music did not stop until 6am. The music was coming from one of the buildings across the road. To put it into perspective, my husband never has any trouble sleeping where ever he goes so for him to be kept awake, well you can imagine! I went to reception the next day and asked the lady behind the desk if the music we had heard on the Friday night was a one off or did it happens every weekend. She looked at me blankly and said that it had not happened before and must have been a special occasion. On Saturday night, the music started to build up from 11,30pm and again did not end until 6am but this time fireworks were also let off. My husband and I could not believe it. Wherever you stay in the hotel, you will not be able to avoid the loud music or the guy talking on the microphone. My husband went to complain the next day. The receptionist advised him that the hotel have complained to the Council regarding the noise but have been told that there is nothing they can do, There were a number of people complaining in the hotel regarding the noise experienced. I am not sure if it is a regular occurrence i.e. if it is a nightclub or it happens every few weeks. On the second night, we even wore ear plugs but could still hear it slightly. The loud bangs from the fireworks woke my son up and not even the ear plugs could shield us from that noise.AC hotel and the Hilton hotel are close by. The AC hotel is even closer to where the music was coming from than Princess hotel!The pool on the 23rd floor was from what I saw mostly for sunbathers and adults. The other pool on floor 3 was shallow and more suitable for children. The water in both pools was very cold and we only managed to go swimming once as he water was freezing. In my opinion, not suitable to swim in. The hotel should have the water heated in the pools.We went to take my son into the Jacuzzi as the pool water was too cold. The Jacuzzi was absolutely discussing. It was a slimy dirty yellow colour. If the jets were on, you would probably not see this and get into the Jacuzzi, god knows what germs and bacteria you pick up!The gym is located on the 3rd floor in a room just off the pool, it was small but adequate.We put a do not disturb sign on our door but the maid still went in and did our room when we were out. On 2 separate occasions, she forgot to put duvet covers on our duvets. The beds are quite comfortable and are on wheels. You can put the brakes on the bed to stop them moving, something we did not discover until our third night.There is a tourist bus which takes you all around Barcelona. This costs around 19 Euros for 1 day or 23 Euros for 2 days. You are provided with earphones and can listen in various languages to interesting facts regarding sites around Barcelona. You can get on and off the tourist bus as many times as you want. You are provided with city maps and a discount booklet. Children under 4 go free on the tourist bus. Be sure to ask what time they stop running. I think it鈥檚 around 8/9pm.The metro and tram are also very easy to use.The shopping mall is right beside the hotel. There are various stores and a big supermarket. If you take any shopping into the supermarket, be aware that you have to place it in a plastic bag and seal it prior to entering the supermarket. There is a table with the plastic bags and a machine to seal it in the supermarket.There are a number of nice places to eat in the mall.The sea is about a 10/15 minute walk away from the hotel. There are no sun loungers on the beach or umbrellas. You can purchase straw mats (2.50 Euros) and umbrellas (4.99 Euros) from the supermarket in the mall. The beach has soft sand and showers to wash off sand when you are finished.In terms of taking food back to the hotel room, we never had any problems with this, we kept ham, butter, yogurts and beer in the fridge and crisps + water on the side. Personally I will not stay at this Hotel again.  
<Date>Jul 24, 2007

<Author>Charl2509
<Content>Best Hotel Ever! My boyfriend and i went to the Barcelona princess for our first holiday and loved it. It was a little out of the centre but the tourist bus stopped right outside the hotel and the trams and metro were less than two minutes walk away. The hotel was very modern and clean. The room was cleaned every day and the mini bar- which was free was restocked everyday too. There are rules regarding taking your own food and drink into the rooms but we didnt find this a problem- we were never stopped taking our purchases upstairs. Our room was the top floor which meant a lift ride up 26 floors- great as the lift was glass and you could see for miles. This was great for views of the Sagrada Familia etc. Room was fairly big with a large comfortable bed, great power shower and blackout blinds and sky TV. Staff were friendly and always willing to help. Room service was avaliable. I would definately book the Barcelona Princess if i return to Barcelona.

<Author>Karenina_7
<Content>Overpriced and impractical Me and my husband honeymooned at the Barcelona Princess this past January for 2 weeks. Given the amount of money we spent on our stay, I can honestly say that it was not worth it. If the price had been half of what it was, perhaps I'd be giving it a slightly better review. To begin with, the hotel is decorated in a very trendy--and therefore often very impractical--way. The front lobby has seating that looks sleek and modern, and that feels very awkward and uncomfortable. The bedroom had a great view (we were overlooking the Mediterranean) but was VERY SMALL and cramped. I don't even know how they expect people to be able to work at the desk that was against the window because the space is so cramped. What upset me most is that we booked a king-sized bed and when we got to the room they had pushed two beds together and figured that wouldn't be a problem (it was our honeymoon for crying out loud). When we complained, they had little to say to resolve the issue. They also don't have an iron and when I requested one, they told me that I needed to purchase one from a store. No iron? Come on.When we were there, one of the saunas was broken and there were problems with the elevator, which is a big problem when you're staying on the 22nd floor. My husband dined at the restaurant there one night (he arrived one night before me) and said that the food was mediocre at best, the portions were tiny, and the price outrageous (which was my impression of lots of places in Barcelona, to tell you the truth--my least favorite thing about the city is the cuisine and its cost). The bathroom is very modern but, again, very cramped. The hairdryer was ridiculously heavy by any person's standards.As for the positives, here they are:1) The hotel is pretty clean and the maid service is very reliable.2) The views from the building are beautiful.3) The train is nearby and very convenient for going downtown or anywhere else.4) The mall next door is very convenient for shopping for food, clothes, dining out, etc.5) The Italian bartender (whose name escapes me--sorry!) was a joy to talk to--he helped us with everything, from advice on restaurants, to how to get around, etc. He was a sweetheart and a consummate professional. We LOVED him.Overall, I don't think the Barcelona Princess is awful. It's a decent hotel, but completely overpriced, especially given that it's not downtown. I would say that it's a good place to stay if you're going on a business trip solo and the company's footing the bill, but as a couple going for a romantic vacation--SKIP IT!However, please don't let this review discourage you from going to Barcelona. Its reputation is well-earned as a remarkably beautiful city with lots of things to do and see. The architecture is breathtaking. Definitely go to Parc Guell, La Sagrada Familia, Tibidabo, Las Ramblas, the aquarium, the omni theatre, etc. My husband and I had an amazing vacation in Barcelona regardless of the hotel being less than we had hoped for.

<Content>Utter Rubbish I booked the Barcelona Princess pretty much based on the reviews I'd read on Trip Advisor and other sites like it, the reviews were typically very good. Well, after a long day roaming what seemed to be the culturally bankrupt city center of Barcelona, my partner and I returned to the hotel with the intention of relaxing in the pool and perhaps taking advantage of the sauna, and Jacuzzi.As we were staying on the 22nd floor, we decided to take the elevator up to the 23rd where there was supposed be a Bar and swimming pool.Well, there WAS a bar, which looked unused and empty, not just devoid of people but of any of the normal bar like things, drinks, glasses, staff! no matter we thought, perhaps we could find some RR in the pool. There was no such luck, the door to the pool was locked. There also seemed to be a prosession of couples looking for the facilities which they'd paid hard earned cash for.Down to the 3rd floor to check out the other pool sauna, and jacuzzi, there we'd find that both Saunas yes that 2 saunas for such a large hotel were both out of order, the Jacuzzi was a third full with some rather strangely coloured water the pool though open was freezing to the touch.I might also add that we bumped into another couple of people from Germany who were also less than impressed, particularly when they'd realised that they paid substantially more than me.After talking to them, we also compared rooms and facilities, it was only on entering their room we realised that the rooms were incredibly tiny and perhaps we'd been lucky with our room on the 22nd floor. Also to their utter horror, the cleaners had placed their belongings in the Bedet!!!! Whether this was a temporary measure while they cleaned the room, this is unclear, however I've never seen anything like this in a modern hotel moreover there was a perfectly good bed where possessions could have been placed during the cleaning of the room.To cut a long story, we all complained to the management about the lack of facilities and poor housekeeping, this didn't seem to register with the guy (once we'd managed to speak to the manager) he thought he could buy us off with cheap champagne and an offer of dinner.Its an appalling hotel, with poor staff, there is no access to the beach, as building work in currently being completed near by, besides the beach is covered in rocks. If you take away one thing from this review it should be this. DO NOT UNDER ANY CIRCUMSTANCES SPEND YOUR MONEY AT THIS PLACE, ITS UTTERLY APPALLING, FORGET THE NICE ONE OFF REVIEWS ITS [--]. I can put it no stronger terms, I'm currenly making a claim through Expedia/ATOL as a result.

<Content>very trendy We stayed here for three nights from 27th April 2007 and we found it to be fantastic. Yes ok there are closer hotels to the city than the location of this one, but lets be honest is it such a hassle to walk for five minutes and then get on the very reliable metro (underground) for another 10 minutes? No. Hotel had great staff was beyond clean and was very open and tastefully decorated. The rooms are awesome with great full wall windows (the black out blinds were brill), the bed was massive and the bathrooms were super cool. I would not really advise this as a hotel for the more mature as i don't think they would really appreciate the lack of privacy of the bathroom but for anyone who is a little less fuddy duddy should go for it. Be warned to make sure the body jets on the shower are turned off before you get in though, or prepare yourself for a cold soakin in your PJ's. Rooms had a free safe and a mini bar with a couple of drinks included in the price. I would highly recommend you stay here but if I was 70 years old and a bit more Victor Meldrew then I would have hated it as it was very modern.

<Content>We Loved The Princess I was a bit worried about staying here after reading some of the horror stories and bad experiences. I can honestly say we had a wonderful stay in this hotel, we didn't really spend an awful lot of time here using it as a base as we were only in Barca for 3 nights.About 10 minutes ride away from Las Ramblas on the Metro and 35 cab ride away from Barcelona Airport. Great location right next to the exhibition centre, shopping centre and huge food hall. Nearest metro 1 minute walk across the road. Quiet part of town, very safe.Lovely modern hotel very clean and minimal decor. 25 floors with 2 pools and a gym. Restaurant and bar open til 1am. 24 hour room service, porter, laundry service and 24 hour reception.We stayed in a superior suite on the 24th floor. Bath, shower, bede, toilet, hairdryer, with fresh towels and robes. Shampoo, soap, razor, shaving cream, nail file, comb, toothbrush and paste.Dressing room space, bedroom and balcony. Huge windows with amazing views of the city. TV, stereo, safe, free internet access (no wifi, conection wires available), phone, mini bar/fridge. Contains 1 beer, 1 small coke, 1 small lemon fizzy non alchoholic drink, 1 small still and 1 small sparkling water.Refilled every day. Shoe cleaner slippers and shoe horn. Smoking rooms/floors and non smoking available. A/C in room controlled by yourself.We loved this hotel, found the staff very friendly and polite. Quick easy check in. Gave us handy maps of the city and metro.Our porter bought up our bags and asked us if we needed anything or wanted info on where to go. Brilliant service.Amazing view from our balcony and in the lift going up. The only thing we didn't like that there wa no iron in the room. We found this very poor. Sadly we had to pay 41.80 euros for an emergency iorning service of 2 shirts a pair of trousers and skirt. Either bring wrinkle free clothes or a travel iron (I usually do bring one). Some other things we found expensive and didn't take advantage of. A tiny bowl of crisps in the bar 3.60 euros, and this one tickled me, ice, 4.80 euros a bucket on the 24 hour room service menu. I guess this tries and stops you from bringing in your own drinks. I would recommend this hotel to couples/singles and business people. We had a lovely stay here, it ticked all the boxes for us for our short stay. I certainly would stay again.Enjoy x

<Content>Issues with room and staff Hi, I stayed in the Barcelona Princess on the 22nd-26th of March 2007. The hotel is a bit out from La Rambla area so if you can find a hotel a little closer for an extra 50Euro I would suggest doing so as the hotel itself had nothing to draw you that far down the metro line unless you are penny pinching.On checkin it went fine, the room seemed fine, on the first day the blind did not work so we were up at dawn with the brightness in the room, they fixed this on the second day (we were there for 4nights). On the day they fixed the blind the safe would not open so we could not get our stuff out to start our tourist stuff. He brought back the safe after about 60mins it was so broke he had to carry it away and either fix it or replace with a good one. On the arrival back on the 3rd day the swipe would not work for us to gain access to the room. We were tired as most tourists are after walking around all day and had dinner booked for that night so wanted to lie down and shower etc. Instead we had to go down to reception where the lady who seemed to be around 30 odd yrs old so should have had more sense, she decided to show a younger staff member how to do it, so train him as we waited, so they made a mistake and now they were training the staff. Held my breath and said thanks and went up the 15floors and once again it didn't work, we went down again at this stage we are not happy as we are home 20mins now and going up and down like looneys. She sent up a guy with us with some special universal key, and once again it would not work so down the 15 floors again. He said it would be 30mins before we could get into the room as he had to get a handy guy. I said this to the orginial lady who seemed to have no empathy with our situation I asked what she suggest we do for 30mins considering we have been trying for 20mins to get in at our expense (up and down 3times) she said wait I asked for a drink of wine in the bar she said no. I asked for the manager she said there was none on duty, to that I said who is in charge if there is a fire and she said there is no fire. So rather than making us more frustrated I decided to say no more and go for a walk, we called back at 21:45 and she said It was open 10mins after we left anyway before we even said anything so we could have exploded with frustration with the receptionist as she was not being constructive or sympathetic. A glass of wine would have kept us relaxed and quiet and you get a complementary beer and coke every day in your fridge (cheap beer) so I can't understand why she was so reluctant to see it from our point of view and give a little.So staff problems with zero empathy is a high chance should anything go wrong. Also it is a bit out making it a pain to go out after touring around during the day and back in for dinner (20-25mins on metro).Also outside of Summer period the upper bar is closedThe pool is very cold.So 4Star in my mind means some empathy with residents but this does not exist.This is why I am giving it a trip advisor two stars=Okay but some problems.

<Author>KrazyKarenT
<Content>Very nice decor We shopped around on the internet and were able to find this beautiful hotel for less than half the price quoted on the Hotel's website. The hotel really is visually stunning! The bathroom has no bath but an amazing shower and sink. The bathroom is separated from the bedroom area by a glass wall which gives the impression of more space than you have. However, if you would like your ablutions to be private there is a blackout blind that can be lowered over the glass wall. The view from our room was spectacular, as was the view near the lifts and on the glass corridor which traverses one tower from the other. beware about the handrail in this corridor though, as both my husband and myself received electric shocks every time we touched it. The minibar contains one each of still water, carbonated water, cola, a lemon drink and beer. This is free and restocked daily. We also got free towelling slippers with the hotel logo on which are quite cute and a nice touch. The toiletries set is the best of any hotel I have stayed in containing shampoo, soap, shower cap, toothbrush and paste, nail file, comb, razor, shaving gel, and shoeshine pad. Noise travels from one room to another. We heard neighbours everytime they flushed the toilet or used the shower. This made us uncomfortable for two reasons. First we were concerned about whether the neighbours could hear our intimate time (!) and second, when flicking through the tv channels, some are very quiet and some are very loud. We didn't do this often though as there were no English channels.The hotel has a restaurant which although is expensive, well worth it. The food is exquisite! The staff in the restaurant were also very nice and efficient.The breakfast room was lovely and the breakfast sublime. They even had soya milk!The staff on the whole were distant and professional. We had no problems with the room or facilities so I cannot comment on how they would handle it. The cleaning staff were excellent.The only negative comment that I would have is that we wanted to buy a cup of coffee from the bar in the lobby and take it to our room. This however was not permitted by the gentleman at the bar. He insisted that we either drink it in the bar or order coffee from room service.Smoking policy:- All public areas are non-smoking (unusual in Spain) but you can request a smoking or non-smoking room on booking.

<Author>Major_Delays
<Content>Great Value for the money We have just returned from a long weekend in Barcelona. After reviewing the options it seemed to be better on the wallet to stay outside the centre and use public transport.The Princess was exactly what we had hoped for, a modern hotel with all the facilities you could ever want, restaurants, gym, pools, bars etc.We found the rooms spacious (jnr suite) and clean. One thing I would mention is the aircon, which seemed a little on the weak side, but when we were there we had no need for it. At 125 Euro per night I felt that we got excellent value for money, but you obviously make some sacifice for that and in this case it would be location, which is perfectly fine, but means a 20 minute journey into and out of the centre each day. The good news is that the hotel is 2 minutewalk from both metro and tram stopsBarcelona has a fantastic public transport system and we found that using the BCN card purchased from the tourist information offices meant we could go almost anywhere we wanted, when we wanted.I would really recommend the hotel if you want to keep your budget under control but still expect high quality accomodation.

<Author>Oscarbud
<Content>Great Hotel After reading some of the reviews of this hotel I'm wondering if I was staying in the same place?.On arrival we was greeted by friendly and helpful reception staff. Our room was on the 17th floor and had fabulous views of the sea. The room was spotless, there was a very large bed with clean, crisp white linen. There is a mini bar with one bottle of coke, beer,lemon and water, which is restocked every day free of charge. There is plenty of wardrobe space also extra drawers and shelves. The glass bathroom does take a little getting used to, but there is an electric blind you can pull down to preserve your modesty if you need to hahaha.The shower is fantastic, and ours never leaked once. Plenty of towels are provided, also bathrobes, slippers and complementary toiletries. there is also a hairdryer. One minor critism is that the TV in the room only has 2 english speaking channels (euro sport and CNN), ok, I know we don't go on holiday to watch TV, but at least one more english channel would have been nice.......(there seemed to be lots of childrens channels ?).We booked room only so I cannot comment on the food, although we did have a sandwich in the corner restaurant on the ground floor which was ok.There is a lage shopping complex right next door and there are various cafes and restaurants on the top floor which were well priced.The hotel is outside of the main town, but there is a bus, tram and metro service just yards from the hotel. i must be honest and say that we used taxis most of the time, and they were reasonably priced.The hotel was busy as Liverpool were playing Barcelona while we was there but there was hardly any noise from other guests.I would recommend this hotel, but remember it is quite a way from the center of Barcelona and apart from the large shopping complex next door there is'nt much else in the area.Just a word of warning........Glass corridors join each side of the floor of the hotel and if you are in your room and the blinds are open people can see right into your room..............just because your on a high floor does'nt mean you cant be seen ?????.

<Author>carlr11
<Content>Great balconies, poor service We have recently returned from the Barcelona Princess. Having read other reviews regarding problems at check in, it wasn't a total surprise that the hotel had no record of the reservation despite doing so through the hotel's own website.After finally getting checked in, we were shown up to the room, which was extremely hot. The air conditioning did not appear to work, so after a call to reception we were informed that the air conditioning system is switched off in the winter. This was despite an efficient system in the public areas of the hotel. This room had some very dubious marks on the wall and was not completely clean. As a result we requested a room change. Eventually the reception staff agreed to show us another room on the same floor which was clean. The second room had a good shower although like other reviewers found, it becomes tedious mopping up the floor everytime. The room had a good if somewhat small balcony overlooking the sea. The hotel pools were open however none were heated contrary to the hotel website. Transport links were good into the city centre with a tram and bus stop directly outside the hotel although it does take sometime to get into the tourist areas.The mini bar is free however, it is only stocked once a day with 1 beer, 2 small bottles of water and a soda!The breakfast was average so no complaints there however on checkout the hotel had charged for breakfast despite the website clearly stating this was included in the tariff. We even queried this with staff on check in. After contact from my credit card company this was refunded but yet another example of poor organisation.

<Author>MPIreland
<Content>Fabulous! My boyfriend and I spent a weekend in this hotel in January (sunny but cold) and we had a fantastic time.Staff were very pleasent and helpfull. The Hotel itself was top class. We stayed on the 22nd floor and the views were out of this world. The room was impressive with a free mini bar that was topped up everyday.The Hotel itself is situated in a quite part of town. Next door is a shopping centre with a huge food court on the 3rd floor which had very reasonably priced restaurants.Getting into the main centre was not a problem as there is a metro stop across the road from the hotel. This goes every 5 minutes and stays going until 2am every night.The Olympic village has a lot of lively bars and night clubs which is just 10 minutes on the metro. La Ramblas which is the main centre of Barcelona is about 12 minutes away from the hotel by metro. It is advisable to purchase a T10 ticket for the metro as this will keep you going all weekend for 6 euro.Barcelona is a must see city and the Barcelona Princess Hotel is the place to stay!!!!

<Author>buzzby
<Content>Awful in many ways!!not My husband and I spent 5 days at the Princess as part of a conference group. The location is terrible. While public transportation is nearby, the hotel is quite a distance from the city center and all the sights. Each taxi ride into the city cost 11-15 Euros. That very quickly added up to much more than we had anticipated.The room was attractjve but small. The bed was very comfortable but the bathroom left much to be desired. The separate shower was next to the separate toilet and the shower leaked onto the floor into the toilet area. Not pleasant. The view was great.The signs in the lobby forbiding guests from bringing in outside drinks or food made it feel like a dorm or a hostel and not a deluxe hotel. Concierge services were non existent and the front desk staff were not knowledgeable or helpful at all. The breakfast buffet was very limited and unexciting.So it seems that what this hotel has going for it are low rates and a modern design look. I would not stay here again.

<Author>HilGray
<Content>Great Location, great room but noisy neighbours We spent three nights at the Princess at the end of November/beginning of December for my husband's 50th Birthday treat.We caught the red eye from Luton so arrived at the hotel not expecting to check in but fully prepared to leave our bags and go out exploring, but the very nice chap checked us in and whispered that we would get a junior suite as the hotel was very full, which was a definite bonus. The room on the 10th Floor had a sitting room with sofa and desk, the main room and a bathroom with shower. We found the room to be clean, of a good size and with plenty of storage space (especially as the sitting room had a wardrobe as well). It is a very modern hotel but we like this style; it may not be for everyone. The views are great (although the bridge between the two halves of the building was a challenge for my husband!).We stayed from Thursday to Sunday and the hotel definitely emptied out at the weekend when all the corporates left.Earlier comments about the noisy neighbours are spot on. At the weekend the local rave venue is very noisy and does go on well in to the early hours. Fortunately we did so much walking we were too exhausted for it to keep us awake but it has to be said that it is extremely noisy and was on every night we were there. We walked to Port Olympic from the hotel which was lovely especially on Sunday morning when the place is buzzing with families, cyclists, roller bladers, etc., enjoying the sunshine.Port Olympic is definitely the place to eat. We would particularly recommend Sylvestre which was very lively with friendly staff and the sea food out of this world. All the restaurants in this complex looked great and were very popular with the locals.Getting around the city is a breeze with the Metro being very efficient, clean and safe. The two day unlimited pass was very good value and very convenient.We had a wonderful weekend at the Princess with the only downside being the noisy neighbours.

<Author>boostravel
<Content>Great Modern Hotel top marks This is a great Hotel, very modern, we went through check in very quickly, our hotel was on the 19th Floor and you would pay top money anywhere in the world to get the view we did, truly fantastic.The rooms are extremely modern and i think you need to like the modern/ urban chic look to really appreciate the hotels style, i know my parents would not like it at all as they appreciate more the traditional scene, i would say this hotel would really appeal to younger people.The metro station is just on the doorstep and the best way to get around, i would advise against trying to walk into the centre, we tried on our first day and what we thought would be a 40- 50 min walk is more like 2 hours and simply not worth it, particularly as the Metro is so efficient and gets you where you want to be in a matter of minutes, its really easy to use, almost identical to Londons Tubes only cleaner and air conditioned.We did not eat in the Hotel, to be honest the menu did not appeal to us at all however next door is the shopping mall with plently of places to eat and Drink, the hotel bar was good though and not too expensive that you feel ripped off, all in all a great value for money hotel.

<Author>thomase
<Content>Good Quality Hotel Just got back from a weekend stay at this hotel which I booked on lastminute.com for my Mum's 60th birthday. Getting to the hotel via taxi was easy and not too expensive, around 拢25.Check-in time was adverstised by lastminute at 2pm and when we arrived we had a bit of a delay in checking in, but it wasnt a major problem. Leaving bags wasnt a problem though. Rooms were nicely furnished and the free mini bar with water and beer was a nice touch (only one bottle of beer a day though!). On the first day we headed into the Diagonal Mar shopping centre which has a great selection of shops, and the bars/restaurants outside on the 3rd floor offer somewhere to handy and reasonably priced to eat and drink if you cant be bothered heading back into the city after a hard days sightseeing!After trying the tram, we found the metro station which was much easier. Buy the T10 which allows you 10 journeys for about 7euros - its good value if you're there for a weekend. The Metro is really simple to use and quick to get to the centre. Didn't try the hotel for breakfast or dinner as there are other options in the cafe opposite or in the shopping centre. The area around the hotel is fine - part residential, part commercial. Some interesting buildings nearby too. Tried the pool on the 23rd floor - nice and warm (even in Oct!). Its a bit of a novelty factor really, but an enjoyable experience.Overall, I would recommend this hotel to anyone who doesn't mind the Metro and wants good value in a nice hotel.

<Author>Jayne-Mark
<Content>Nessun Dorma.... The Barcelona Princess is an ultra-modern hotel a couple of miles out of the city. The shopping centre next door has a variety of OK restaurants  bars  the adjacent Forum Conference Centre, surrounded by a huge concrete park and marina, makes for an interesting location. Some correspondents have commented on the showers - I enjoyed the multi-jet experience, though mopping up afterwards due to the ill-fitting door became tiresome. There are some terrific aspects from the lifts  high rooms, and with some more welcoming staff the hotel could move from good to great but for one thing outside its immediate control...'Espacio Movistar'. Adjacent to the Conference Centre, this marquee-like music venue pumped out rave at a volume sufficient to rattle the glasses on the shelf in our 18th floor room until 5am on Saturday morning....even my ipod at high volume in my ears couldn't drown out the beat. Reception were sympathetic (saying they had called on the police to intervene) but could offer no help, nor, when I asked them the following morning, a change of room (the hotel being full and anywhere 'it won't make much difference'). The following night's prog rock was better - it wasn't as loud and finished at 4am - but still cost us several hours' sleep. If you're thinking of going to this hotel at the weekend, unless you're deaf, a raver or the hotel have assured you there's nothing on down the road - don't.

<Content>Very good value We have just returned from staying at this hotel and found it to be very good value for money. The room we had was very comfortable, with a huge bed. We had a lovely view of the sea and made use of the electric blinds. Plenty of toiletries and the free minibar was very handy. The shower was a bit daunting to begin with but we soon discovered if you adjusted the showerhead, that solved the problems. We thought it would have been more helpful if there had been more drawer space. However, we managed. If the green line had been operational it would have made a big difference to us for getting around, this stops in September. We used the tram and the metro which was a very slight hassle to reach the tourist bus. We were so tired with all the sightseeing that we would go to the shopping mall to eat before returning to the hotel. The choice of restaurants was great and suited us just fine. The downside of this hotel was not being able to bring food in. We thought this rule was a bit ridiculous, especially with there being a superb supermarket in the mall. Ok this hotel was not in the main centre, but it was a lovely hotel, very comfortable, quiet and made a very relaxing break for us. We would go back again.

<Author>reggy123
<Content>Not Bad - could have been better I stayed at the Barcelona Princess Hotel on business in mid-October and here are my comments.On arrival it looks an impressive building, out in suburbs with quite a lot of building work going on around the hotel.We had a delayed check in by an hour or so, (system failure) conceirge offered free drinks which was a nice touch. Finally got to room and air-con was broke, took 2 hours to fix. Free Mini bar not replaced every day. Being a smoker in a smoking room you expect an ashtray, NO! Asked at reception and was told to use a drinking glass instead as they don't have them!!!!Room was clean enough with a great view of the city. Watch out for the shower, it leaked under the seal and flooded the bathroom!! Uber modern, or trying to be so not the most functional room you'll ever stay in.The lifts were a nightmare, only 3 and with the hotel being full it took upwards of 5 minutes waiting going up or down at times....badly designed! Only ate breakfast once and once was enough, good selection but the food was lukewarm at best and expensive.Staff in general were efficient if not that friendly except the two guys working in the foyer bar. Both were more than helpful and very friendly, they make some excellent cocktails as well :)Ideal location for business trip, convention centre across the way and superb shopping centre Diagonal Mar right next door. Good tapas to be had here! About 20 mins from Las Ramblas etc, centre of town. Tram was confusing at first but got the hang of it, trams stops right outside the hotel. Metro at Glorias stop takes you all over the city but be prepared with your map and expect a few line changes.Too conclude our stay we took the tourist bus around the city, excellent value and an ideal way to spend your day. Nou Camp was fantastic as was Port Olympic, good food and night life.Good hotel but as I say, it could and should have been better for a superior 4 star (as advertised). Probably won't stay again but it served the purpose well enough.Finally, watch your wallet as two guys had theirs pick-pocketed within yards of the hotel!!!

<Author>VuittonFanatic
<Content>our best accomodation during our 3-wk trip around europe my friend and i decided to semi-backpack around europe earlier this year. what i mean by semi backpack is 3* hotels and up... no motels... and absolutely no hostels. average price of our hotels was around U$ 100/night. we were planning to stay in barcelona for 5 days and 4 nights... therefore, we feel like we could compromise on this hotel's not-so-central location. of course, several dissapointed comments on this hotel got us worried. but, we decided that like everything in life, it is most likely a 50/50 chance... so, we booked all of our 5 days and 4 nights accomodations at the princess.we arrived in barcelona late afternoon. figuring out the location to this hotel is a bit tricky. i think in expedia, it mentioned the nearest metro station was diagonal mar. well, hello... there's a diagonal metro... but no diagonal mar. we asked the tourist info at the sants' station (main train station at barcelona) and she told us that the hotel is quite far out, about 30-40 minutes train ride from sants... and it is near diagonal mar MALL. duh! once we arrived, there were 2 exits (to the street level)... we took the wrong one and ended up walking quite a bit, compared to if we've taken the other exit (sorry readers, cant remember exactly which exit to take... but if i remember correctly, it's the kind that you'd have to take a lift to go up to the street level). the street lighting is quite dim at night... so for single girl traveller, i would suggest going home early or bring some kind of a defensive tool, just in case... since we bumped into several drunk people on several nights (i guess they party hard in spain). ok, about the hotel... there were 2 other people in front of us and the darn front desk took their sweet time, not even acknowledging our existence. we just got off a 7-hr train ride... a smile, an apology or a quick check-in service would have been nice. even after he was done checking in the other people, he curtly told us to wait for another 5 minutes. but the coolness of our room, totally made up for the lack of courtesy of the front desk officer. i cant believe we got such a great deal for our money! our room is super duper clean, none of that gross smell of smoke, the tables are clean, the window glasses are immaculate. we love it!!!we went downstairs to get suggestions on where to eat and the 'other' front desk person suggested the next-door mall (diagonal mar) since we rather not go anywhere far. at the top of the mall, was this open-air food court thing that's fabulous. we ate most of our dinner at this chinese restaurant, china guo. the food is good considering you're paying like 3 euros for a sumptous size vegetable fried rice. definitely a perfect restaurant for on-the-budget traveler. the waiters are nice and accomodating. if you've been to europe, you know what a rip-off dining out (or buying anything, in general) can be. oh, buy your water from the grocery inside the mall... SUPER DUPER CHEAP! but remember to hide it as you're entering the hotel and keep them inside your luggage. since the hotel has a policy where they reserve the right to charge you extra for bringing outside food and drinks. but, buy your water/juices from this mall before you head out to the city. save you tons of euros.GOOD THING abt this hotel: real great value. this is our best accomodation in the entire trip ($100/night budget, 3 countries, 9 cities)... clean. safe. mid to upper-class guests. the maid CLEANS the shower everyday... love that you can get free wireless internet! they have this ultra cool, great pictures, great descriptions guide book in our hotel room that really helps in planning our trip around the city.BAD THING abt this hotel: it is quite far out from the central of the city. but if you have plenty of time... if you can afford wasting a little time riding the metro, this is the place! it is close to the olympic village where the better food at more expensive price tags are. at night, around the hotel you have nothing... but the restaurants on the top of the mall (since people in spain dont eat dinner before 9pm). THINGS TO REMEMBER: every frickin' mall in spain/europe, in general closed on sundays... so plan your trip accordingly. visit sagrada familia EARLY in the morning... yeah, its a pain to wake up early, but its a bitch to wait in line for 1.5 hours. remember, it takes abt 40 minutes to get to city center by metro... bon voyage...

<Author>Celtictiger
<Content>Nice Quirky Hotel Princess Hotel Diagonal Mar, BarcelonaThe Princess Hotel Diagonal Mar is a Modern / Stylish hotel in a new area called Diagonal Mar near the Forum , this area was formerly an industrial area. The hotel is 4 star quality with glass walls between the En Suite and the Bedroom, but there is also an electronic curtain that can be let down. It is a tall building approx. 24 floors beside a Good Shopping Centre called Diagonal Mar, which in my poor spanish indicates that it is at the end of the Diagonal street at the Sea. The Hotel is modern and while we had a view from our high floor we could not see the sea. The hotel lacks the ambience of an Intercontinental or Crowne Plaza.I would recommend it for Business or First Time Honeymoon Couples but only for a few days. We later moved to the Barcelo Atenia Mar which was near overlooking the beach, not as quirky but comfortable . The price of the Princess Hotel fluctuates so check your dates. We did not use the restaurant for breakfast as it is over priced. The housekeeping was excellent

<Author>alli
<Content>Very Disappointed My husband was attending a conference and I tagged along. the hotel was chosen by the event planners. The rooms looked like the web site. I have to say that it seemed like little thought went into the functionality of the design. You enter though the bathroom which is ok but it is all glass. Remember to close the bathroom blinds. The shape of the building is such that people walking down the hall can look right into your room. The views are very good but I had to keep the blinds drawn most of the time. The shower is great looking though again not well thought out. The shower heads face the shower door. Not thinking I turned the water on and got a direct hit. There is no way to let the water warm without getting sprayed. Plus the shower door is flush with the floor and did not seal correctly. Each time we showered we flooded the room. During our stay it rained heavily. Most of the hallways had water coming in. They had towels down lining the hallways in an attempt to stop the water from coming in. I found the staff to be disinterested at best. The only good thing I can say is it is a good location for attending a conference but if your traveling for fun I'd stay elsewhere.

<Author>kiddo74
<Content>Very nice, close to mall and the beach My husband and I got a great deal at Barcelona Princess when we booked our stay early, 2 nights for a total of 160 euros. We were nicely greated and given a room on the 25. floor. We did not see the ocean, but had a great view of Sagrada Familia and the city. This came in handy when there was an amazing fireworks show our first night!Our room was nice, very quiet/soundproof, big bed, cool interior design and free minibar.The hotel is close to the beautiful beach, approx 10 minutes walk. The third positive thing with the hotel is that you can catch the metro from the station Maresme, only 2 minutes walk. Even at 35 degrees it was freezing, so we could just keep it on for shorter periods and not during the night. We told the hotel about this, but it was not fixed.It was also a bit disappointing that the pool area on the 23. floor was closed for maintenance. <Author>audi21
<Content>Must Be A 5* I am not being snobbish but i have been to many 5* hotels around the world, and to think this hotel is not 5* is just incredible. It is in fact considered 4* superior and is very good at that. The rooms are very modern and clean. The staff were very polite and helpful and assisted us whenever possible. We arrived to the hotel at 12pm and requested a high floor room. We were told our room would be ready at 1pm so we went to have lunch on the beach, leaving behind our luggage in the hotel. We returned to the hotel at 2pm and were given a sea view room on the 25th floor. We were told that the minibar was free which included coke, lemonade,a beer, still water and sparkling water. The room was lovely. I have been to Barcelona twice before and stayed in 4* hotels and the rooms were much smaller that this one. The shower was powerful and massaging.It was a true pleasure to be in the hotel room and looked forward to coming back to the room. The only negative point i think is the tv which had 30 channels, but the only 3 english channels are CNN,bloomberg and eurosport. The blinds in the room are great, and make the room pitch black and difficult to wake up in the morning, so have an alarm ready to wake you up every morning.There are 2 computers in the first floor which we found always empty and used for the internet, but there is internet available in each room so thats another bonus. Hotel location can be annoying after a while. The tram is an easy way to reach the beach taking about 10mins and the metro takes 12-15mins to the centre. Overall, i cannot stress enough how impressed i am with this hotel and would definately stay there again.

<Author>Silent Crow
<Content>very upscale feel The Barcelona Princess is a wonderful hotel. The rooms are extraordinary in that the views are spectacular, and the features within the room are divine, right down to the faucets. Some of the rooms actually have balconies, and though those rooms don't have DIRECT ocean views, they give you a span of Barcelona well worth the (moderate) price of the hotel. Those same rooms are larger than the ocean view rooms, with a much more unique layout.  The spa facilities are filled with young (attractive) visitors on holiday, and the pool itself, at the top of the roof, seems like an ad for Hedonism, with all the sun bathers. Had I not been there on business, I too would have whiled away many hours taking advantage of the tremendous spa facilities. The breakfast is actually one of the best I've ever had. It is, like 90% of hotel breakfasts, a buffet, but the choices are extraordinary. In reading the reviews before choosing the hotel, I had a couple concerns about the attitude of the staff. There were very few moments when I felt the staff wasn't exemplary. One has to know and understand Spain a bit to understand the attitude. No one is likely to get preferential treatment, but everyone is going to get great service. (I was able to check in when I arrived before noon, but I was only lucky.) The only complaint I have is not against the hotel itself. The location is not terribly accomodating if you're on holiday. It's great for the convention center, and it's great if you want to go to the mall. BUT, if you're in Barcelona to experience classic Barcelona, I would look to stay elsewhere. Otherwise, you'll be exhausted just getting around. For business, or a holiday with teenagers who want to hang around the hotel while YOU go experience Barcelona, it's perfect. Brilliant, in fact.

<Author>PM62
<Content>Great Hotel and Excelent Value We stayed for two nights over a weekend and I could find little if anything to criticise the hotel for. We arrived around midday and as our room was ready they allowed us check in early, and met our request for a high floor with a city view.The rooms are very modern and a bit 'Austin Powers' with the electric blinds and the glass wall between the bedroom and the bathroom and the 'trick' shower, but all very nicely done. The free minibar (one of each of a beer, coke, lemonade, still and sparking water each day) was a nice touch.Although the hotel appears to be a fair way out of town, it is only 15 minutes by tube. There is a tube station just around the corner, and both the normal and tourist buses stop right outside.As this is a 'business' hotel, the rates drop dramatically on Saturday and Sunday, and the reduced weekend rates are a steal.

<Author>emma_1980
<Content>Loved the view, not the stairs!! We chose the Barcelona Princess largely due to a lot of good reviews on the Trip Advisor website and everything we read was true . . .We arrived at 11am and couldn't check in until 2pm but were able to leave our luggage at reception. The staff spoke good English and this was hassle free.Our room was on the 26th floor, at the top, magnificent views over Barcelona and the sea. The room was definately the best we've stayed in - very clean, stylish and yes, the shower is unbelievable!!The hotel is a 20 minute tube ride to the city centre - we found the easiest way to get around was the tube, and purchased a metro ticket that enabled us to make 10 journeys for just under 7 euros. The metro tickets can be purchased from a ticket booth which has English instructions. The only downside of the hotel was that on our last night in Barcelona there was torrential rain and the lifts in hotel were out of order. We had to walk up 26 flights of stairs to get to our room without an apology or any explanation from the staff - their customer service could definately be improved!!

<Author>BriL
<Content>Excellent Hotel My husband and I have just returned from Barcelona and we both agree that this hotel was great. We stayed for 7 nights and this was a perfect length of time to enjoy all that Barcelona offered. The rooms were extremely clean and very modem and the free minibar was a nice touch as there is a strict policy against bringing your own food / drink into the hotel (although a rucksack did come in useful!!). Th shopping centre beside the hotel is good and there are also plenty of places to eat out in. There is also a metro about 2 minutes from the hotel and a taxi to the Olympic Port is only about 6 euros. It is worthwhile taking the Tourist Bus which leaves from outside the hotel as it takes you all around Barcelona and you can on and off it as often as you like.

<Author>clarabubs
<Content>Would definitely recommend! I visited this hotel with several of my friends (for my best friend's hen-do) in August 05. We had booked via the internet and got a really low rate so weren't expecting much. We were delighted with what we found. The hotel was immaculate, stylish, air-conditioned and the staff were very pleasant and helpful. It's a little out of the way in relation to the city centre but there's a bus stop next to the hotel, a metro station nearby and reception were able to call taxis within a few minutes for us. We decided to jump on the hop-on/hop-off tour bus which takes you all round the tourist sites in Barcelona and were very pleased to find that one of the stops is outside the hotel....very convenient. There's also a sizeable shopping centre right next tour with a great selection of fashion stores, restaurants, bars and a supermarket. Ideal for our group!The only down-side was the lack of balconies. I'm not sure if the larger, more expensive suites have balconies, but ours didn't - just a huge window with electric roller blinds. Would have been nice to be able to sit out on a balcony, but the view was great nonetheless!Would definitely recommend this hotel to anyone and I hope to return again soon!

<Author>alegna1
<Content>Wonderful views from room at night Booked thru Booking. Stayed 3 nights at the Princess. Travelled with my 3 kids (11,13,15). When they saw the hotel there were screams of delight. Impressive. Great views from our 14th floor rooms, which compensated for not having a sea-view. Great Location, but a 20 minute tram ride to the centre (Las Ramblas) or at least a 35 min walk. Tram stops outside the hotel.Tourist bus stops outside hotel! The tourist tickets can be bought from the hotel desk although it's odd that you have to pay for the 5 Euro voucher offered (?) by the hotel. The hotel receptionist insisted that it was a reduction, but this isn't true. It's the same price if you buy from the hotel or directly from the tourist bus. (But the hotel probably takes a commission !)The free mini bar was welcome, although room service forgot to replenish after the first night. This was corrected when we reported to the desk.The design bathrooms are lovely and the rooms large and nicely designed. Slippres and bathrobes are welcome gesture.The two pools are tiny but adequate. The view from the pool on the 26th floor is, needless to say, splendid.There's a shopping shopping centre next door where you can eat reasonably priced meals. We always ate breakfast there. Lots of different restaurants. Eating out in Spain is not expensive and the salads are delicious.Smooth and friendly check-in/out.Enjoyed our stay. One of the nicest 4 star hotels I've stayed at. :-)

<Author>Alison36
<Content>fabulous hotel great hotel in a lovely quiet area. easy to reach by train and metro but takes about 1 hour - loads cheaper than a taxi though. We used the metro system a lot and found it to be very reliable, clean, cheap and safe. On checking in at the hotel, we had to leave 150 euros as a deposit as we don't have a credit card so be prepared before you go for that. Other than that couldn't fault the hotel or staff. Rooms are fantastic, pool gets a bit crowded so late afternoon we went for a 5 minute stroll to the promenade for a couple of hours - no beach, a wooden decked area, very safe, clean and cool with the sea breeze. <Author>Tripper8
<Content>Loved this hotel- definitely going back My family and I stayed in this lovely hotel in July 2006for 3 days before embarking on a Mediterranean cruise.I had read the reviews on Trip Advisor, and they were very accurate. The mini fridge is stocked with beer, lemonadeand pop each day , and is free. I had a large bedroomfacing the sea on the 20th floor and the view was great.The room is very modern, the King sized bed was comfortable,the room darkening blinds were very effective. Only 2 peopleper room - even little kids can't stay in the room with you. Mysister has 2 small kids and she had to book a separate roomfor them. But my entire family (15 or us in total ) loved this hotel.The shower cubicle is separate from the toilet cubicle for eachroom. The kids (and I ) loved the shower- all over body shower.The toilet cubicle could be a problem for larger sized people ,and for claustrophobic people because the door goes upalmost to the ceiling so you have the sensation of being closed up. The toiletry area is outside the shower andtoilet cubicles.There is a room safe for valuables. The only negative is the security staff is very strangely adamantabout not bringing in any outside food. I had read this on a review before I left, and it was true. My mother was stopped and questionned about her bottled water which I thought wasridiculous.We had a wonderful dinner in the hotel restaurant on my lastevening. The portions were small but very tasty.The beach is nearby - walking distance. There is a largeshopping mall with lots of places to eat just a few stepsfrom the hotel. The tourist bus goes by outside the hotel.We bought a 2 day pass, and hopped on and off the bus.Pay attention to the routes though .I will definitely go back to this hotel.

<Author>Warm Weather Traveler
<Content>Barcelona Princess will blow you away before or after your cruise! As always when using a discount site, I was nervous about this hotel, especially when I got a $95 each room rate for two rooms on Expedia for my wife, myself, and our two teenagers. Not only did they get us adjoining rooms, they were adjoining on a high floor.We stay in 5-star places (Grand Wailea, Atlantis, etc.) in great suites, and this was easily a set of rooms worth $400+ combined. Like the rest of Barcelona, the design is amazing, and if you are a gadget person, you'll love the power window shades, power screen room dividers over the glass wall to the bathroom, cool showerhead system, free unlimited internet, wake up call built into the TV, decent cable, etc. The only thing you may want to do that we didn't is bring the two prong adaptors and voltage regulators, but they did provide (I brought an ethernet cable with me, but they provide that, too).We had nearly 10 bags and they were courteous about storing them for 2 hours until our room was ready at noon. The staff was universally courteous, and sent two guys that loaded us IN our cab for the airport the next day as fast as an Indy pit crew.If you have tiny kids, you might want something less avante garde, but for teenagers, the chic pools, free stocked minibars, $10 euro cabfares to Olympic Village or Avenidas Ramblas, etc., made this the wonderful surprise of the week. You are also just a block from the Hilton, next door to a very nice mall, and a very short walk to the largest public beach in town.BOOK THIS NOW before other people hear of this first class hotel posing as only a 3-star! If I ever go back to Barcelona, I'm all over this place! You will not be disappointed!

<Author>nixfromlondon
<Content>Fantastic place for a city break! I stayed in this hotel with my boyfriend for 3 nights at the end of a fortnight's holiday in Spain - and really loved it. Having visited barcelona before and been stuck in a souless hotel out by the airport, we had wanted to stay in the city centre but found prices too expensive. This hotel is a great compromise - it's just a short taxi/metro ride from the centre, and you get much more for your money than in a city centre hotel. It's a really chic modern building and the rooms are fantastic: spacious and equipped with all mod cons. We had an amazing view over the coast, which was only beaten by the view from the open-air pool which is virtually on the roof of the hotel! We didn't eat breakfast as it seemed quite pricey, but found plenty of places nearby instead. Overall - I'd definitely recommend this hotel - and will be back there whenever I'm next in Barcelona!
