<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great Rooms and Views We stayed here from the 8 July for 4 nights, two adults and a 9 year old boy having spent a week in a sister hotel in Cap Salou. We booked a Junior Suite and were given an adjoining room for Cameron, we in fact had a Junior Suite with another room next door (both of our doors were seperated from the rest of the corridor by a seperate door which should have enabled to leave our room doors open but could not be locked despite requests to reception). However Cameron enjoyed his King Size bed and all the electric blinds etc, he had the shower and we had the bath/shower. Our room had the balcony which was cornered and had a Sea and a City view especially from the 22 Floor (rooms 2207 and 2206). The rooms and servicing were excellent even though the mini bar is a bit bare as described in other reviews. There is the food police to stop you bringing food into the hotel but it is signposted but you just put it in a ruckSack or fancy shopping bag (Burgerking in an Armani bag). The shopping mall next door has a good variety of eateries from Sushi, Italian through to McDonalds and Subway but the shops are not anything special. There is a supermarket type shop that has great food stuff in the mall I bought some cold nibbly snacks but they were intercepted at the door, I was given a receipt and was told that they would be refridgerated until my departure the next day, they were a touch on the warm side and I did not risk it. The bar was a bit steep at 6 Euros for a Gin and the mixer was 2/3 Euros more, city centre prices in an outskirt hotel. To be honest the infastructure around the hotel allows easy transport by all means from the doorstep. In summary, love the hotel rooms, staff could be more helpful, silly food policy and steep bar, the two pools 1 on 23rd floor is about 50 ft long and 4 feet wide for the swimmers, and the one on the 3rd floor is a triangle shape suitable for kids and a cool dip. Some rooms are at the end of a glass floored corridor but it is opaque glass, not exactly the walk of faith, but it feels a bit strange. You either love or hate the view from the lift, some people did face the doors at all times.

<Author>shelbyandcecils-mom
<Content>Not as we expected We selected this hotel based in part on the reviews here, but also on the fact that we were staying in another hotel in a different city that is part of the same chain. We reserved 4 rooms for our group for a three night stay in Barcelona. The rooms were as discussed, beds comfortable and the blackout shades a necessity on the ocean view side of the hotel. The views from all of our rooms was nice. Be warned however that the shower temperature is very difficult to regulate. I was almost scalded several times without ever moving the temperature lever. It seemed to lessen if you turned the water on and left it running for about 10 minutes or so before getting in (what a waste of water), but the temperature was never consistent. We had also requested that one of the rooms have a bathtub. Fortunately, we were able to switch rooms around amongst ourselves to accomodate this need, but there is apparently only one room per floor that actually has a tub. The free minibar is misleading, there is one water with gas, one without, one Coke, one beer and one lemonade, per day period. Another review has noted the guard standing in the hotel lobby. Guests are not permitted to bring any food or drink into the hotel. At all. We found this to be very unreasonable. We drink lots of water. Some of our group were older and in the heat needed to stay hydrated. Needless to say, we found this to be a problem. We were also told that we could get a glass of ice from the bar. That worked on two occasions, on the third, the bartender refused. We were told to call roomservice for ice and they would bring it to our room. We then did so three different times...and we were given two different sized of ice buckets and charged three different prices, the largest being 5 euros. Outrageous for ice. The air conditioning in one of the rooms did not work, it was reported to the front desk. A man came and said that he fixed it, it continued to not work. The second day in the morning it was reported again. That afternoon, it required another visit to the front desk and a reminder that this was a 4 star hotel and perhaps they needed to increase their level of service to a 4 star level, that the airconditioning was finally fixed. In general, only one or two of the front desk staff spoke English, and not well, no Italian and only a little French. The breakfast buffet was complete, but at 17 euros, not a good value. There are several shops, cafes in the mall next door that are just fine. On a positive note, the laundry in the bottom floor of the mall did a terrific job on laundry, and a much better price than the hotel's quoted 4 euro for a pair of underwear price. Nice pressing of the gentlemans' and ladies' shirts and blouses too. Somehow, with them not speaking English and us not speaking Spanish we managed to have a great discussion and get our clothes done appropriately, unlike attempting to converse with the front desk staff. The tour bus does stop outside the hotel, and that was a reasonable way to become acquainted with the city. We spent the equivalent of 12 nights in this hotel, reservations made for us by a Spainish business associate and felt that it was not up to 4 star standards in the slightest.

<Author>goglu
<Content>great room, great service, fabulous views! We stayed at the Princess hotel from June 17th to 24th. We arrived early in the morning, and could not get our room until 1:00 pm. This was fine with us, as we spent a few hours walking along the coast up to Port Vell (approx. 20-25 minutes walk). We were given a room on the 25th floor, where the view was absolutely spectacular! The room was even nicer looking than on the pictures, and all features were working perfectly (electric blinds, super shower, etc). We enjoyed the bathrobes and slippers, the free mini bar, and the room was always kept spotless, although they did come late in the afternoon to clean it. After two days, we would hang the make-up the room sign on the door when we left in the morning, so they came earlier the following days.The hotel is out of the center, but the metro station is only a 2 minutes walk from the hotel. The station is Maresme y Forum. Use the metro if you are spending a few days in Barcelona, it is very cheap, efficient and safe.The reception staff was always professional, but I admit they were a little limited in giving informations. Some of them spoke french which was a pleasant surprise for us. We rented a car for one day to go to Torres winery, and they made all the arrangements for us. The car was brought to the hotel early in the morning, and we just had to bring it back at night. No hassle going to a Hertz counter, or finding parking.If you want a little quietness in the afternoon, use the 3rd floor pool. Lots of chairs, a little music, a bar, and it is never crowded. We were often only 3-4 person by the pool, as there is no sun at the end of the day. The 23rd floor pool however offers a great view of the sea, and has sun until about 6:00 pm. There are only about 10 chairs and they are always taken.Be warned, they do not allow you to bring food in the room. There is a guard at the door, and if you come in with a supermarket bag in your hand, they will purely refuse to let you in. We had an opaque carry-on bag in which we put a few things for breakfast, so we were able to bring that up to our room without any problem.We strongly recommend this hotel, which does deserve its 4 stars. We have travelled often to Europe and this is now one of our favorite places.Have fun!

<Author>JustUsTwoDerby_UK
<Content>Amazing Hotel, Amazing Price I booked the hotel through a last minute deal and was really impressed with the service and hotel from the moment we arrived. First of a taxi direct from barcelona airport to the hotel was only just over 30 Euros. For the convenience we thought this was great. Because of an early flight we arrived at the hotel around 10:30am (check in is from 3pm). But when we spoke to reception they said they would see if we could check in earlier. 5 minutes later we were in our room unpacking. But that isn't all because we had booked a really cheap deal (拢200 for 4 nights), although I had asked for a room on a high floor I wasn't holding out a lot of hope, well I was wrong our room was actually on the 26th floor......(You can't get any higher than that).Throughout our stay we found the staff to be really friendly and the hotel was lovely, only thing we heard people say they were disappointed with were the pools. We weren't disappointed though because they look small on all the pictures from the barcelona princess website.The hotel bar was expensive compared to anywhere else we visited (but again you kind of expect that). On our last day they weren't able to allow us a late check out room (we did not need to leave the hotel until gone 7pm. However, they informed us that we could still use the full hotel facilities so we could shower and change in the Gym - so no problems there.Overall one of the nicest hotels we have stayed in (even compared to some 5 stars), location a little out but we actually liked that as right next to open top Tourist Bus stop and also Tram and Metro.We would recommend the hotel 100%, just one word of warning about Barcelona - pick pockets are rife. We were lucky - despite a couple of attempts on my wifes handbag (which we managed to foil) we didn't get anything stolen. But a couple of women staying in our hotel got handbags snatched apparently hotel staff said it happens a lot. So you have to be very careful and security conscious...... But it shouldn't spoil a beautiful city break.

<Author>melsriver
<Content>Overall enjoyed stay, but comes with warnings A group of ten of us stayed at the hotel Princess for 5 days May 31st-June 5th. Overall we had a great time. Will give a brief description of the good and the bad:THE GOOD: Checkin went very smoothly, we arrived at about 10:30 am and check in was not until three, but we were all in our rooms within the hour. The rooms for the most part were great. The black out blinds make it hard to wake up but very easy to fall asleep We were on the 24th floor so the view was fantastic! The beds were also very comfortable and the mini bar was a great touch as well! The shower was fantastic! It has the spray nozzles that spray out on different body parts! very enjoyable! Being right next door to the shopping mall was great, we ate lunch outside on the roof one day, and that was quite enjoyable, we also got some food and beer for our room from the huge supermarket! That worked out very well! Having the tram right there and the metro one block away was great as well, we were a 10 minute metro ride from Las Ramblas and the Olympic Port, keep in mind the metro stops at 12:00 so you will have to take a taxi back to the hotel.Ok now for the BAD:Two out of the five rooms we had were missing doors, one on the shower and one on the toilet. Now if you are a couple this might not be so bad, but we had two friends staying in both these rooms so it made it quite difficult. The two girls staying in one room, complained about not having a shower door and were laughed at and told that some rooms did and some rooms didn't have doors. Well as I explained above the showers have those sprayers that spray out, without a door you would not be able to use them! They were eventually moved to a different room and everything was fine Now for the REALLY BAD, not altogether the hotels fault!!!The weekend of June 2nd-5th there was a huge music festival across the street from the hotel. It went until 6:00am one night, This made it very difficult to sleep if you were on the side facing the festival. My parents complained several times during the night and actaully checked out one night early to go on to Sitges because of the lack of sleep.The genreal manager was very nice in helping them get moved and offered to pay for their night in Sitges, however since it was booked through Expedia we shall see if it works.However the next morning when the rest of the group checked out no one was compensated anything even though we all complained about the lack of sleep due to the festival.Final word of advice: The Princess has a few quirks to work out but overall we enjoyed our stay and would probalby go back as long as we checked to see if any festivals were going on! Make sure you ask the hotel if any events are planned at the forum during your stay!One other piece of advice I highly recommend for everyone. Right outside the hotel is a bus stop for the Bus Turistica. It takes you all over Barcelona to see everything you would want. you can buy a daily pass or a two day pass. You can hop on and off the bus wherever you want. Great way to see all of Barcelona. We hopped on and off at our convenience and it was great.Also look into the multi day metro passes you will need those also!

<Author>ajhaeh
<Content>Goods to Declare - Beware We stayed with friends at the Princess for three nights and reading the reviews prior to visiting it appeared that there was no middle ground. Either people loved it or hated it. Well I'm somewhere in the middle and my report will be balanced. The thing that stood out for me above all the rest is that the hotel, for us, was not customer focused. Well certainly not 'holiday' customer focused. From the moment we checked in it appeared that we were 'privelged' to be staying at the hotel and the reception staff were efficient but assertive. We had rooms on the 4th floor overlooking the Forum and this hotel is not on the sea front as a previous correspondent has written. You are a good walk from the beach over car parks and two main roads. There is construction work at an industrial complex about 1/2 mile away which is near the sea front. The hotel is on the corner of Avenue Diagonal, it is number 1.The rooms are very spacious, modern and open plan. There is a complimentary mini bar of four soft drinks and a beer. The power shower is good but when on full blast the drains couldn't cope which resulted in the flooding of the bathroom area. (The same happened in our friends room). There are electronic blinds on the huge window and also blinds between the bathroom and bedroom. There is also a door between the two rooms for privacy. The walls are not too thick between you and next door and with Pete Doherty playing until the early hours of the morning next door to the Forum... there were a couple of noisy sleepless nights.The events of day two are quite farcical and bizzare. Next door to the hotel is a shopping mall, with a host of shops and supermarkets. I purchased some water, fruit juice and some potato crisps to nibble in the room. As I entered the hotel I was stopped by a receptionist who had been instructed by the manager (who was stood at reception). Well my bag was confiscated!! It was highly embarrasing and I felt like a naughty boy in the headmasters office. All the other customers were watching as my bag was taken away to a side room and I could collect it on departure. I could not beleive it. I complained to the manager who stated that it was 'rules' and indicated a small sign at reception. It did say a small fee was payable if you wanted extra items in your room... 50 Euro's! The night after the sign became bigger and was placed by the lift. The reception staff were then placed on guard duty taking bags off people as they came in. It was like going through customs with the 'Goods to declare' channel. Farsical! The confiscated items were placed in a room and when you went to collect them it was a free for all. Bizarre! However some people were lucky enough to get away with the draconian measures and take beer wine  spirits to their room when the staff were busy. Crazy.We got a great rate of 拢58 per room on Expedia and many correspondents have outlined the transport systems to down town Barca. The price is really half what it should be for the quality of the rooms, as the hotel is just two years old. We did visit the Hilton Diagonal Mar across the street and had a fantastic meal in the Indigo Restaurant. The food and service were first class. The Princess manager needs to visit to see how it should be done... but who am I to say, I am only a customer and I should be grateful for allowing the Princess to let me stay... Shouldn't I :-)

<Content>A true Princess! My wife and I stayed in the Barcelona Princess for 3 nites in late May 06. We booked it with [--], about 鈧?00 for 3 nites!..Like most previous reviewers, i was a little apprehensive about the somewhat varied reviews.Yes, the hotel is a 15 minute Metro ride from the city centre, but the top floor view we had of the entire city more than made up for this. Room service was prompt and surprisingly tasty and fairly ok with regards price. The air con worked perfectly and was a must.The only negative comment was the constant humming noise, which i reckoned came from some sort of air con motor on the roof..but we were the closest room to this, being on the 26th floor, and besides we got used to it after a while.All in all..i would totally recommend this hotel and you will get far more value and quality than what you pay for.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Only for business travelers My husband and I stayed at the Princess while he attended a conference in Barcelona from May 5-12, 2006. We would choose a hotel closer to the center of town with friendlier staff and more comfortable facitlites if ever we returned to Barcelona. The metro station is a two minute walk from the hotel, but it's a 20 minute ride to the center of the old town and farther to other tourist sights in the city. The rooms were very modern, but dark, and the beds are quite firm. The bathroom is separated from the room by a glass wall, and the toilet has no door- so no privacy there! We had a view of the sea, over the top of an industrial area (so really not very scenic). A room key is needed to turn on the electricity for the room. This is not unusual in modern hotels, but what caused us trouble was that the window shades were electric, and when my husband accidentally took both room keys with him, I was left in the pitch dark unable to open the curtains (bring a flashlight!). The staff was often not helpful, and sometimes even bordered on rude. We never did succeed in convincing the maids to let us use the extra pillows in the room, each day they took away the pillow cases and stored the pillows. Breakfast was a full buffet with a decent variety of fruits, pastries, meats, eggs and vegetables, but the quality was just average- sometimes the pastries were stale, usually the juice was sour.

<Author>Hally1982
<Content>It truly is fit for a Princess We, being my girlfriend and I, stayed at the Princess Hotel for three nights, Sat to Mon.After reading some of the extreme range of views posted on this website, we were a little apprehensive. <Content>Wonderful Hotel, spent our 5 year wedding anniversary here! My husband and I are from Massachusetts and were visiting my husbands family in Ireland for 2 weeks. While in Ireland we booked a 3 day/2 nite visit to Barcelona to celebrate our 5 year wedding anniversary. We were in the Barcelona Princess May 4th, 2006 evening and May 5th, 2006 evening. We loved the Barcelona Princess and only paid $106 per nite from hotels(--) You would never find a hotel of this quality at that price in Massachusetts, or most other places in the USA or Europe. We were on the 11th floor and had a view of the Mediterannean. The room darkening shades were great! The first morning I woke up and it was pitch black in the room so I thought it was 4am..turned out it was almost 9am!There were a bunch of young English Tourists on a trip and were very loud in the bar. As the other reviewers pointed out, yes it's a mile or so away from the city center but the subway is right outside the Barcelona Princess. We had a 2 day Barcelona pass so we used the subway which was very convenient. I worked out on the outdoor stairmaster one day which wasn't a great stairclimber but it was okay. I didn't go in the pool but some of the English tourists were in there. The Sky Bar at the top was closed.I would recommend the Barcelona Princess. It's a great deal for the price. However as someone else wrote, the rooms may be a bit too modern. It took us awhile to figure out some of the light switches/shade controls.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Don't bother if you are looking for a 4 star hotel I booked this hotel following the reviews on this website and have to say that I was not overly impressed.If you are looking for a four star hotel this will not meet your expectations. The hotel was fully booked because it was a bank holiday weekend but that is no excuse for the poor (and often rude) service.The double room I had booked 4 months in advance turned out to be two single beds pushed together. The hotel staff were most unhelpful when I pointed out that I had booked a double. The receptionist told me to speak to the manager. When I asked to be put through she told me that manager would not be available until the next day. The issue was never resolved.Some of the facilities the hotel claims to have were not working. The Jacuzzi didn't work and the person in charge told me to report it to reception if I wanted to use it. The Jacuzzi and swimming pools did not look like they had been cleaned for a while - with hindsight I was glad the Jacuzzi was not working!I wasn't impressed with the rooms either. Although we had a sea view the room was clearly visible by people using the bridge to the other side of the building. This meant that we had to keep the blinds drawn most of the time. Coupled with the black ceiling and blind over the glass bathroom wall most of the times the room was very dark.It's hard to think of any plus points. My overall feeling was that I would not stay there again unless all the other hotels in barcelona were fully booked.At most I would award this hotel 3 stars.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Brilliant Just got back from this hotel and would certainly recommend to all. Its not in the city centre but the metro station which is a 5 minute walk takes you there in about 15 minutes and costs peanuts. Taxi back in the evenings was around 8 euros. We did walk into the city centre and it was a lovely walk. Took about 1 hour walk to the Olympic Village then a further 45 mins to the centre (Ramblas). Theres also another port there with a shopping complex. If you come out of the hotel and walk towards the sea theres the beach and theres even a lovely walkway to walk all the way into the city centre. (Ah yes...the first beach is a nudist beach....you have been warned). The hotel itself is very modern and stylish. Although it had all the amenities, we didnt use them. We stayed on the 23rd floor overlooking the city and at night when lit up...the views are amazing. There is a shopping centre next door to the hotel and certainly gives you a few hours to kill, its also full of restaurants inside and outside. We didnt pay much per night at this hotel (easter break) probably 拢60 per night and it was worth it. If I was to go back to Barcelona I would definitely book this hotel.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fantastic Hotel If you are afraid of heights, do not stay at this hotel unless of course you're on the 6th floor or below.There's masses of glass and floor to ceiling windows. Glass elevators, glass walkways and of course the infamous glass bathrooms.Getting to the pool on the 23rd floor was a no-no for me due to the height/glass walkway issue but I hear that it's very nice.The reception staff were incredibly helpful and polite and check-in was efficient and quick.The one and only negative comment would have to be about the shower. The temperature fluctuated from freezing cold to scalding hot and that was without even turning the tap sometimes.The blackout blinds in the rooms and the largest beds that I've ever slept in definately made for a restful night. The free mini-bar was a really nice touch as well.All in all, a great hotel and coupled with the excellent transport links on it's doorstep (metro, tram and buses - including the tourist bus that stops right outside the door) it's definately worth a visit.

<Author>mierman1
<Content>Bad Attitude I booked my room in Barcelona based on the raves on this webpage. I figured I'd sacrifice prime location for a luxury stay. However......First, we did not get the room that we booked. We booked a double room but instead got a twin. They fixed this by pushing the beds together. This might have been ok without the staff's rude take it or leave it attitude.Second, many of the so-called attractions of the hotel closed early (or maybe were never open). Twice we went up to the 23rd floor bar to have a drink and enjoy the view and it was never open, even during hours it was scheduled to be open 10.30 through 20.00.But most frustrating was the staff being rude, possibly even deliberately. Twice we asked for simple directions, such as the best way to get downtown, and was told incomplete and even WRONG information. We were told to get on the tram in the opposite direction and transfer train lines. This is completely unnecessary as the Metro is just around the corner - we just couldn't see it at first. (Note: if you are staying here, it is unlikely that you should need to take a tram). Later, we asked a different person if a bus would have been a more direct route to where we were going and we were given a curt yes without giving us which bus line to take and we ended up going all over the city. We also saw staff members giving condescending looks to a group of tourists that were just having fun.In short, the location ended up being ok with the proximity to the Metro, but the staff was so unfriendly and unaccomodating that I would not recommend staying here.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Excellent hotel Just returned from spending 6 nights. I decided to stay here with my wife based on the reviews in tripadviser. I cannot recommend this hotel highly enough. Yes, it's a little out of the way but it is only 15mins from the city centre on the metro(which is very easy and cheap to use, and is only 2 minutes walk from the hotel). It took us 20 mins to walk to the Olympic marina along some lovely beaches. There is some redevelopment and building work in the near vicinity but it really is not an issue. I also cannot comment on the food as we were not prepared to pay the hotel prices, it seems to be the same in all of the Barcelona hotels - very expensive. There is a large selection of eating places next door in the shopping mall. Also there is a cash machine which accepts any type of card, with no charges, just past the entrance to the mall. I won't go on too much about the hotel as its all been written before - it really is lovely. The rooms are very impressive. Remember to ask for a city view as high up as you can get. Our room was cleaned every day and was spotless,plus we got clean towels,bathrobes and slippers daily. They even give you a daily selection of soft drinks in the free mini bar.We had people on either side of our room but we could not hear a thing apart from the blinds being used.A few extra things worth a mention. This is our 2nd visit to Barcelona and we have not encountered any problems with petty crime. If you are sensible and careful it's a safe city - just have your wits about you. The locals in tourist areas speak mostly good English and are friendly and courteous.Try the seafood restaurants around the Olympic marina - spectacular.Have a wander up to Camp Nou on match days and you will be able to buy tickets for the football game. I went up and got tickets for the Benfica match;even my wife enjoyed the fantastic atmosphere in the stadium.The Barcelona Princess is lovely - look no further if you want a good base to explore the city with the added bonus of access to the beach when the sun is shining and you need a rest from all the sightseeing.

<Author>Janeite
<Content>Sooo quiet! As others have noted, this hotel is a little out of the way for the major Barca sights. We considered that a plus. We could easily reach the city center by subway or taxi, then sleep peacefully all night. Our room was very quiet.The room was comfortable, if a little odd. The wardrobe is painted black inside and is in a dark part of the room, making it rather difficult to find one's black clothing. We actually used a flashlight. Drawer space was inadequate for two people who overpacked, but we made it work. The free minibar was nice, and telephone charges very reasonable.The bathroom sink is glass. Very pretty, but always looked dingy after we used it, esp. as no soap dish is provided. The shower is truly a treat.Other facilities were mixed. The jacuzzi was out of order throughout our stay (though there were men pounding on it, so perhaps it has been repaired). The sauna was lovely, but again dark--the only light was provided by the glass in the door. There were showers in the changing room, but no soap, shampoo, etc., and the showers were so small it was easy to switch off the water with a shoulder or elbow. There's a small massage room, where I received a very good and very reasonably-priced massage. We did not use the pools but they looked pretty.Breakfast was included in our package. It included a nice range of fruit, cereals, cold meats, yogurt, breads, etc. It also included some tired-looking vegetables probably left over from dinner. Coffee and juices were good. We didn't try any other meals. As others have noted, very good shopping is just next door. Cava at 2 euros a bottle, anyone?

<Content>Lovely hotel, very modern We stayed at the hotel for three nights. Staff were very helpful; we had no Spanish at all, and had some difficulty with directions etc. They made every effort to help us.Rooms were spotless, with fantastic views of either the city or the sea. Free minibar stocked every day, bathrobes, slippers etc provided. Safe included in the room.The hotel is a little bit out of the city, but is still only a 10-15 min metro trip. For a livelier atmosphere, it's probably too far out, but the hotel itself is very good. The Diagonal Mar shopping centre is beside the hotel, and has two floors of shops, and one of restaurants/cafes. I would stay at the hotel again; it's lovely.

<Author>mascarasnake
<Content>Glassed Bathroom March 2006 - 4 of us stayed here for a long weekend, we had adjoining rooms which was great. Check in was a little slow as was check out - staff were friendly but slow. The bar staff went out of their way to make our stay memorable, nothing was too much trouble for them. As all hotels the drinks here were more expensive than bars - about 40% more. Breakfast was not included in our rate-we were charged 16 euros each. The selection was fresh fruit, cold meats and cheese, hot grill, cereals,toast,muffins etc. It was as one would expect from a 4* hotel.Dont get too excited about the swimming pools, they are very small but welcoming for a quick dip after a long day sightseeing. This hotel is a 10 euro taxi ride into the centre. Near the hotel was a shopping mall. If I return to Barcelona for a short stay I would choose a hotel a little nearer the centre, but this is an individual choice.The hotel bedroom was very clean, and the bathroom a little different with a glass partition dividing this area from the bedroom - we were on a high floor with spectacular views of the city.

<Author>cass1410
<Content>loved the hotel but not the location Stayed here for 2 nights whilst the football was on. Found the staff very friendly, on check-in we were offered a sea or city view room. We chose a cityview and were located on 24th floor - the views are amazing! The room itself was lovely, spacious, very comfy bed, the minibar was included in the room rate with water coke and beer which was refilled every day. The bathrooms were a bit odd. There is a glass partition between the bathroom and the bedroom which there is a blind to pull down but our room didnt have a door to the toilet! the shower had 3 settings with small and large jets and I loved the bathrobe and slippers.Room service was pricey, one night we tried for 15 minutes to order food and noone answered the phone.The location is the only thing that let this hotel down. The public transport is great and there is a bus and tram stop just down the road but if you want to be in the action dont choose this hotel. It takes a good 15/20 minutes by public transport to get to the ramblas and costs 10 euros by cab.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Fantastic views This hotel is fantastic. We arrived for a 4 night break at around 11 o'clock and were pleasantly surprised to be able to check in instantly. Not only that, we were offered a high or low room with city or sea views. If the same choice is offered take the high option with a city view. It's fantastic in daylight but as the sun goes down the panoramic views just get better. The room itself was extremely clean with black out blinds that leave you wondering where the morning went as they're that effective. The other plus point is the fantastic shower.Admittedly the location is out of the centre, but it's about 15 minutes on the metro. For the metro there are various options such as 1, 2, 3 or 4 day tickets available. This however is purely for the metro, whereas the T10, the ten journey tickets can be used for bus, tram or the metro which gives more flexibility. Overall if I was to go back to Barcelona I'd happily go back to the Barcelona Princess

<Author>quiltingtravelmom
<Content>What a treat! Our family usually stays in budget hotels to cut the cost of travelling. But, thanks to your reviews, we were able to spend just a bit more and be totally pampered at this wonderful hotel. I travelled with 3 teenaged girls and we all loved the bathrobes, slippers, and girly stuff provided. The shower was a nice start to each day. The views from the hotel are wonderful. Even from the elevator! There were two computers available for free internet access, but I found it difficult to get a turn. You would be better off bringing your own laptop.The beds are large and very comfortable. The all-glass bathrooms are beautiful, but if you want more privacy, there are shades that can be lowered and a door that can be closed.We ordered room service two nights for a special treat. It was a bit pricey, but the steak especially was perfect. Not many vegetables on the menu, though. Free minibar was nice, but there is only 1 Coke, 1 still water, 1 fizzy water, 1 fizzy lemonade, and 1 beer per day. Still it was good to have.The hotel is on the far side of the city (on the Med), so out of the hubbub of the city. The shopping centre next door is actually one of the largest shopping malls in Europe!If you use public transportation, there are two bus lines that stop at practically the front door as well as a new tran. The Metro station is just a short walk away. I highly recommend this hotel.

<Author>2HpyTravelers
<Content>Modern Barcelona We stayed in the Barcelona Princess for one night before departing on a cruise through southern Europe. The room was reasonably priced and very modern in style. After the long flight from New York, the BLACKOUT blinds in the room made our midmorning sleep refreshing. The room was smaller than a standard American room, but very comfortable. Hotel staff members seemed nice and helped to minimize the language barrier. My wife managed to flood the bathroom shower (in her defense the drain was slow) around midnight, but the hotel staff quickly responded to soak up our sixth floor Lake Victoria. The exercise facility was small and horribly appointed and the pools are tiny, but those amenities were not factored into our choice of hotel. We would definitely stay at the Barcelona Princess again in the same situation. If we were going to Barcelona to stay there for a week or two, we would stay somewhere else.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>awesome! Amazing very modern hotel suitable for all kinds of visotors, we stayed on the 18th floor with a city view which was amazing, especially at night time when the whole city was lit up, the rooms very beyond comfortable and offered many great things such as free mini-bard which was topped up daily free of charge with water, beer, coke, etc. The rooms were cleaned daily and towels replaced, free television with about 30 chanels including sky news and mtv. The shower was great very powerful with 3 different settings, the bathroom is all glass and silver and looks amazing and is seperated from the bedroom by electric blinds which were great! the electric blinds for the window were great as well as they offer complete darkness if you fancy a few winks. the kingsize bed was very comfortable as well! The hotel as is the whole city no smoking (apart from a few small bars/cafes) so if you smoke like me you have to go outside, or alternatively theres a nice little bar directly opposite the hotel called la rambla which allows you to smoke and also sells very cheap beer and does food as well. The metro and tram are both outside the hotel and the metro is about 7 stops into the city centre, be careful though as one british tourist standing next to us got her purse stolen out of her bag on the metro when it was busy, the pickpockets are very clever when doing it. The room service however was poor, very expensive, poor portions and the food wasnt all that great. Amazing city and an amazing hotel!

<Content>Great Trip I recently stayed at the Barcelona Princess with 5 girlfriends. We had a fantastic weekend. The hotel is very modern and lovely and what stunning views you see from your hotel bedroom. The swimming pool on the 23rd floor was a bit cold as its outdoor but well worth a look. <Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Great quiet location I stayed at this hotel for 3 nights with my boyfriend and could not be more thrilled with our choice. The check-in was quick and easy and the room was lovely and tidy, with amazing views. The house keeping was spot on and the shower is simply devine. Furniture and decor is very modern, with a nice european chic about it. As mentioned before, the electronic blackout blinds are great, but be warned that it does make you oversleep! The location of the hotel is nicely situated outside the hustle and bustle of the city centre. However, do not let this put you off, as the Metro station (Maresme Forum) is less than a 3 minute walk from the hotel. The Metro is very convienient and is about a 10 minute journey to the city centre and many other attractions, such as Sagrada Familia, La Rambla and L'Aquarium. The hotel also facilitates a sauna, jacuzzi and two swimming pools. Massages are also available for about 50 Euros. My boyfriend said the massage was superb and almost fell asleep! The room service is fast and not hugely expensive. There is always a security guard at the door, which is a nice safety precaution. Though, I'm sure he is not really needed as the area is pleasent and quiet. The hotel staff are friendly and helpful, although with limited English, but they do try and help in anyway they can. There is a big shopping centre 2 minutes away and has everything you need. Many restaurants are located on the 3rd floor of the mall, with a wide selection to choose from. I would highly recommend going to Araguil, which is a tasty Lebanese restaurant.

<Content>Overall Great Value This hotel was a great value: Good price (about $100 a night from Expedia), close access to Metro, Clean, Nice Views, and a free minibar. The Bathroom was very European. The tub had glass that covered only half way so there was a lot of water splashes on the floor (being an American, this is one of my pet peeves about European showers). There were no face towels. They provided a free toothbrush, shaver, shower cap, shampoo, and soap.We arrived on a Thursday and the taxi cost us 鈧?5 Euro. We checked out on a Sunday and the taxi cost of 鈧?5 Euro. Apparently, there are two tariff rates. One for Monday - Friday. And a more expensive rate for Saturday and Sunday. Plus, there is a 鈧? Euro charge for the airport and 鈧?90 charge for luggage...so don't freak out when you see the fare start at 鈧?.90. The closest metro station is Maresme-Forum. When you exit out of the hotel, cross the street and continue straight two minutes. The metro station will be on your left. There is also a mall next door to the hotel called El Diagonal Mar with many restaurants. The food at Pizza Marzano was really good!

<Author>ludiandrade
<Content>Great Hotel Stayed at the Princess Barcelona on Nov 3-5, 2005 prior to sailing on our Mediterannean cruise on RCCL Splendour of the Seas. We had a beautiful view of the city from our 16th floor room. Execellent hotel. Very European decor. Extremely modern  clean rooms. Professional and very pleasant staff. Excellent service. Security at front lobby door 24 hours. Food is pricey, but you can go across the street to the Ramblas and have a good breakfast for a fourth of the cost. All that is in the room fridge is complimentary - so is the bathrobe and slippers - they don't tell you that upon check-in. Free high-speed internet is offered on the second floor. Hotel is adjacent to a large mall you can walk to. It is not centrally located but you can easily reach the center by train. Taxi from airport to hotel is about $25USD. Always negotiate the price of the taxi fare before accepting. We were robbed by the cabbie from the hotel to the ship-port - charged us $70USD. Would definitely return and recommend this hotel. Book it with confidence!

<Author>waterstone
<Content>Clean and modern Overall, the Princess is a nice hotel. I stayed in a double room, which I thought was quite large for a European hotel room. The furnishings were contemporary and the linens and towels excellent. The bathroom was relatively small and didn't have a tub (though I can do without a tub). Housekeeping kept the whole thing spotless.The blackout blinds were a nice touch, as was the very much appreciated free minibar (soft drinks, water and beer, 5 bottles total per day, and included in the cost of the room!).The EUR 16 breakfast, though a little steeply priced, was a hefty buffet with hot and cold items. And of quite good quality.The front desk staff were a little hurried and not especially friendly, but not unpleasant either.The only major drawback to the hotel is its location in El Maresme. It's next to the giant (yet mostly unexciting) Diagonal Mar mall, but is otherwise in a primarily residential (and equally unexciting) neighborhood. But the inexpensive and reliable metro is close by, and the real Barcelona just a 15-minute ride away.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Definately going back to the Princess! What can I say? What a great hotel! My boyfriend and I stayed here for 5 nights. It was my first time in Barcelona, it was my 18th birthday and my 2 year anniversary with my boyfriend, and the Barcelona Princess Hotel was the icing on the cake! It's everything I expected and more! The decor was fantastic, the rooms were clean and modern but cosy. We were on the 18th floor - 1808 was our room! It was lush! It had a lovely view of The Forum and the sea, it was so tranquil waking up to that view every morning. The shower was heaven! The free minibar was a great plus, and the complimentary toilets were really good too. Bathrobes and free slippers! The room service was quick. The staff were very helpful about the local area, where to dine, how to get to places from the hotel and etc. There's a lounge area (Dali) just above recpetion which has 2 computers with internet access - very handy if you don't own a laptop. Going up and down the lift is an experience itself! From the gorund floor to the top floor you can see EVERYTHING bit by bit, floor by floor! It's amazing!My boyfriend and I felt very cared for during our stay at the hotel which was very nice and welcoming. We had breakfast at the cafe opposite the hotel entrance 'La Rambla' it was delicious! 2 slices of toast, 2 rashers of bacon, 2 eggs and a fresh orange juice was about 5 Euros per person. We also went to the shopping centre next door, Diagonal Mar for breakfast/lunch/dinner. They have everything in there! Subway, pizzerias, Dunkin' Donuts, tapas, fresh smoothie stall, crepes, Ben and Jerry's, Japanese... the list goes on! It's great for shopping too. Transport links are really good, the metro stop is across the road about a 2 minute walk from the hotel, the tram and bus stop is just a few metres down the road from the hotel. By metro it only takes about 15 mins to Passeig de Gracia which is the city centre. Port Olympic is only about 7-10 minutes away by metro, it has many restaurants, bars and a huge casino. We found a restaurant we really liked at Port Olympic called 'La Fonda', the receptionist recommended it to us. It is mainly seafood but it serves all sorts, the food is gorgeous!! We bought 2 5 day Barcelona Cards for 60 Euros. It gives you unlimited transport on the metro and bus, and discounts to attractions, museums, the aerobus (airport bus), restaurants and shops. It gives you a metro map, bus map and a street map of Barcelona.So to sum it all up, Barcelona Princess is great and we WILL definately stay there again and again! I will put my photos up when I get them processed!

<Author>zoris
<Content>What a fabulous hotel! Following extensive research on Trip Advisor I decided to book the Princess for a surprise holiday for my boyfriend and I was not disappointed - it far exceeded my every expectation! The staff were friendly and we were checked in quickly. We had a gorgeous, very spacious suite on the 19th floor with fantastic views of the sea and the city! The bathroom (which had a luxurious feel with bath and shower) and seating area were large, absolutely spotless and the towels/bathrobes/toiletries etc were fabulous. The bed was large and extremely comfortable. The balcony was great with windows/glass spotlessly clean. The blackout curtains guaranteed a good nights sleep and the room was very quiet with no noise being heard from other guests. The free stocked mini bar was also handy! We found the location great, the metro being over the road and only a 10 minute journey into the heart of everything you could wish for. Port Olympica was only a 5 minute journey away and a good night out (but if you don't like seafood, you may struggle for choice). Our taxi was 25 euros from the airport. Breakfast in the hotel was expensive but I was prepared for that and Starbucks in the shopping mall next door solved that problem! The hotel bar was very relaxing and the bar staff really friendly and welcoming.To sum up - a fabulous hotel, one of the best we've ever stayed in and ideal for a romantic get away - I thoroughly recommend it to everyone!

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Poor Service The Hotel Barcelona Princess was clean and modern as depicted on the various websites we searched. HOWEVER, my boyfriend and I had trouble figuring out why the entire hotel staff was not accommodating in the very least. For a so-called 4-star hotel, the staff (manager, and receptionists included), were discourteous and rude. We addressed staff in both Spanish and English and did not find them to be any more friendly as a result of our efforts. The hotel manager was especially obnoxious, imposing a phone tariff and dirty looks for a meager LOCAL call we placed to a friend informing him that we would be stranded for 1/2 day out of our 3 day excursion OVER SEAS. This was definitely a huge discomfort and left a very bad taste in our mouths, along with the absurdly overpriced $16 Euro breakfast. BE WARE: taxis from the hotel to other parts of the city include an automatic excess fee of 5 EUROs as the hotel imposes it on the drivers. You should not encounter problems in any case as staff will never lower themselves to calling one for you.

<Author>gm2484
<Content>Just satisfactory We chose to stay in the Princess because the children were offered a free connecting room. This was great as they had their own room, bathroom and facilities. I found the staff pleasant and helpful, though as pointed out in previous postings, slow to book in. But we were on our holidays and time was not a problem.The rooms are very dark , quite small but clean . Our shower leaked all over the bathroom floor, so much so that we had to use quite a lot of the towels to soak it up. Yes, we too had the knob inside the toilet stuck on with selotape!! But the toiletries were lovely, towels spotless and fluffy and replaced everyday. The pool was very cold and never seemed to have the sun shinning on it. I realised quite quickly why no one was in the water or sunbathing. The pool area was in the shade most of the time. The seating in the bar area was faded and had seen better days.The location of the hotel is 15 mins by metro from the centre. We are well used to travelling so this was not a problem. The shopping centre next door had the whole floor of eating places with lots of choices. We enjoyed seeing how the local people lived and their children playing in the little play areas. There was a huge play area both inside the shopping mall and acroos the way beside the Forum which kept the children happy.We enjoyed our stay at the Princess but if going back to Barcelona would stay somewhere more central. Hope this helps anyone making a decision as whether to stay or not.

<Content>Fantastic value 4* Having stayed in a large number of 4* and 5* hotels in resorts and on business I can honestly say that this is the best 4* I have stayed at in a long time. Rooms were not huge but of a fair size for a city break. Small touches like free soft drink and beer in the minibar and slippers and dressing gowns are things that are sadly becomming increasingly rare in this class of hotel, but not here! Also, the unique glass bathroom wall makes the hotel different (blinds come down if you're shy!) and the power shower has to be seen to be believed. More something you would have in your home than a hotel!We booked direct with the hotel and would recommend that you do this as the rate was very reasonable doing it this way. Three nights cost us about 鈧?40. Don't get breakfast in the hotel, the caf茅's in the shopping centre next door are good.It is true that the hotel is a bit out of town, but taxi's are inexpensive after midnight and the tube service is fantastic.I would recommend that you get a taxi to/from the airport as with luggage getting the train then tube is not worth the hassle. it is at max about 鈧?5 euros in a cab.We booked the day before arrival and did not request a high floor with a view until arrival and were still lucky to get the 21st floor. Recommend this hotel and room 2102.

<Author>Iain____Mitchell
<Content>Fantastic City, Wonderful Hotel We stayed in this hotel in September 2005 for 11 nights. We arrived at Barcelona Airport late afternoon and caught a train from the airport to Sant Adria del Besos (4 euro each taking approx 30mins) Since the tram outside this station wasn't operating we got on a bus that was put on instead, and this dropped us off outside the hotel. Taxi Fare would have been 30 euro. We took advantage of a room on the 22nd floor which provided breathtaking views of the city. The room was modern and clean. Facilities included air conditioning, pc point with free internet access for those with their own laptop, television, safe, and minibar providing 5 free drinks daily (1 beer, 1 coke, 1 lemon and 2 water). We were slightly dissapointed that the large double bed was in fact 2 single beds pushed together but they were joined by brackets so didn't come away from each other. The hotel pools were very small however as we were rarely in the hotel we would not have been in a position to use them anyway. We did use the sauna which was again very clean and free towels provided. Across from the hotel entrance about 75metres is the underground station El Maresme/Forum(Line 4) and I would recommend you buy a T 10 given 10 rides on the underground system. NB The underground closes at 12am Mon-Thurs but is open until 2am at weekends. Taxis are reasonably inexpensive so if you have ventured into the city centre it doesn't cost a fortune to get back to the hotel in the early hours. Barcelona has so much to offer from a sandy beach to gothic architecture to modern art. The hotel offers free internet access from 2 pc's on the 1st floor and this is useful for finding out places of interest or local restaurants whilst you are there. The hotel bar is well stocked and nice for a quiet drink although did lack a bit of atmosphere. Olympic Port is only 30minutes walking distance for those looking for a more lively nightime scene. Overall a modern, clean and friendly hotel and we will definetly consider staying there on our next Barcelona visit.  
<Date>Sep 17, 2005

<Author>R-LIL'S
<Content>Princess of all hotels... This hotel is in a great location called the Forum and what a fantastic hotel...nice, clean, friendly and very near the beach. The staff were very helpful and very friendly and they all spoke English. I was here for six days with my boyfriend, this being our third visit to Barcelona this year. Our room was on the 25th floor with fantastic views of the sea and Barcelona skyline. Our room was very modern with a free mini-bar (5 drinks free each day) and a glass bathroom with black-out drapes, very useful if your shy.... The hotel was very clean, and everything was provided including slippers, nail file,shaving kit and a toothbrush (I forgot mine). The sandy beach Nova Mar Bella was only 10 minutes walk away with several very cheap bars open until all hours. The famous Port Olimpic was an enjoyable 20 minutes walk away, the restaurants and clubs in Port Olympic are well worth a visit, something to suit all ages. The nearby tram was not working however the metro was very easy to use.The hotel bar was rather expensive (鈧?8 for 2 drinks) so we visited the shopping mall next door where we got a bottle of Torres Brandy for 鈧? and several bottles of chardonnay for a cheap 鈧? per bottles...lovely jubbly. There was also some lovely places to eat here including a fantastic tapas cafe...well worth a visit.The outdoor pool on the 23rd floor could be seen from our room -there were only about 10 sun-lounges available. There was also a small pool on the 3rd floor with more lounges available. The nearby Parc de Diagonal Mar (park) was very romantic and peaceful. Barcelona is a fantastic City, this is our third visit this year and we will be back....we love this city and this hotel tops them all - we will return.

<Author>touchango
<Content>Great Views Over the City!! I stayed at this hotel with my boyfriend over New Year (which coincided with my 40th!). I surfed the web for quite a while before booking and booked this as it seemed to be a great standard hotel for a very reasonable price. I noted that the best views were undoubtably going to be from the high floors so asked for a room on a high floor when I booked over the net.When we got there we drove round the block twice as we couldn't see anywhere to park before it became evident that everyone just dumped their car in the road outside and gave the keys to the check-in desk for valet parking. Parking fee was extra but not too expensive.On check-in we were asked if we wanted a sea or city view and opted for the city view. We were given a room on the 25th floor with spectacular views over Barcelona at night. The room itself was great and very clean, and the free mini-bar was restocked daily. Loved the bathroom and the electric blinds!We didn't have breakfast at the hotel as it was quite expensive but there were very inexpensive places to have a coffee and a pastry in the shopping centre next door. We did eat in the hotel restaurant one night (New Year's Eve) but they ran out of food (it was buffet style) so it wasn't spectacular and I wouldn't recommend the restaurant. We did complain about the meal the following day (we couldn't complain on the night as too many people were complaining already!) and spoke to the hotel manager who gave me his card and asked me to email him when I got back (but I never got round to it).There was internet access in the lobby which was great for keeping up with emails. We didn't use the pools as it was January but although small they looked quite nice, especially the infinity pool on the 23rd floor!The hotel isn't in the greatest area but they seem to be doing a lot of building work in the area so maybe it will be nicer soon, but it's very near the metro which is very convenient for seeing the centry of Barcelona.I would definitely recommend the hotel and would stay there again.

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>luxe for less We two sisters and mothers of young children booked this hotel because it had two pools, was near to public transport (Maresme/El Forum on the yellow line towards La Pau - strangely the tramvia was not working along the Avignuda Diagonal while we were there and no-one could tell us why) and was remarkably cheap for a 4* hotel. We were all delighted - by the free minibar, the artemide tolomeo lamps, the blinds, the glassy bathroom, the lovely chambermaids and hall porters, the dinky but very pleasant pools and terraces. It is an amazing package. When I booked, I did wonder about some of the earlier complaints - Fawlty Towers, etc, but frankly, unless you are a top-exec type, who can't bear to wait around in reception for 20 minutes or so while they work out their computers, you will have no complaints.We didn't try the breakfast or restaurant/room service here because of the price, and because Barcelona is full of characterful places to eat. The Gym Bar was good for lunchtime sandwiches and drinks and all the staff were polite and helpful. It was quite funny to see a notice by the lift which threatened supplementary charges for people who brought in food from outside, but the huge Diagonal Mar mall next door, full of fast-food restaurants was a bit of a mixed blessing for the proprietors of this hotel as I saw people bringing in their Burger Kings in a brown paper bag. Probably not the image the management was looking for when it invested in the Moroso and BB Italia lobby furniture. The Canary Wharf type regeneration that is going on locally makes the spot quite soulless but calm in comparison with the hullaballoo of the historical centre - it was relaxing to come back late at night to a spacious and dust-free environment. Public transport is extremely cheap - 6.9 euros for ten trips on bus/metro, which can be used by the whole party. Taxis are also good value - about 28 euros to the airport and around 8 euros to the centre of town. We really enjoyed the hotel and the holiday as a whole. The only bad shock was a 63 euro phone call to China, but that's not compulsory.  
<Date>Aug 4, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Excellent Hotel with an Excellent Location Just returned from a 2 night break in Barcelona staying at the Hotel Barcelona Princess. This hotel was very clean, comfortable and modern with excellent facilities and the staff were all very helpful. On arrival at the hotel we were met by a porter who later brought our luggage to the room and answered any questions about the hotel. In our room there was plenty of information about the hotel and city attractions. We were staying on the ninth floor and had a fantastic view of the sea. The minibar was complementary and was re-stocked upon request and room service was also available 24 hours. On our first night our shower leaked over the bathroom floor but within 20 minutes a maintenance person came to the room and resolved the problem.I had been worried when booking the hotel that we would be too far from any of the main attractions but we were just minutes from the beach (making the temperature more bearable) and there was a huge shopping centre right next to the hotel with plenty of shops, bars and restaurants. The hotel was also located right next to metro station which is a very easy and cheap way of getting around the city (the metro trains are also air conditioned). To sum up I thought the hotel was fantastic but 2 nights is not long enough in this amazing city. I will certainly be going back and will definitely stay at the Hotel Barcelona Princess again.  
<Date>Jul 20, 2005

<Author>A TripAdvisor Member
<Content>Loved It! This is a fabulous 4 star hotel. I was a little worried about it being too far from the buzz of Barcelona but this is a great hotel in a great location. Don't waste money on taxi's from the airport - follow Expedia's advice and get the airport train to Sant Adria de Besos Station and then get the tram to the Forum [about 3 or 4 stops] and the hotel is just across the road.We didn't try the food at the hotel so cannot comment but the Diagonal Mar shopping centre which is directly next door has everything from Starbucks to Pizza plus it also has a supermarket which sells EVERYTHING!The hotel rooms are fantastic - great air conditioning [very quiet], blackout blinds [fantastic], great views and spotlessly clean.Buy a 10 trip ticket which can be used on the underground and trams - this was a great deal and saves times as well as money.We didn't realise that the beach was only about 10 minutes from the hotel and you can walk [which we did most mornings] along the coast line to the centre of Barcelona [takes about an hour but worth it].I would definately recommend this fantastic hotel.  
<Date>Jul 5, 2005

<Author>LindseyCulley
<Content>View to die for My husband and I stayed for 4 nights. I booked through 2 different companies 2 nights with each which worked out cheaper and didn't have to change rooms half way through which was good. B/fast was included for the first 2 but was pricey to pay for the second 2 at 16 Euros each, so didn't bother. Modern rooms with the most spectacular view of Barcelona, we stayed on 23rd floor and I would recommend to anyone to stay above say floor 15 to appreciate the view available. Shower in the room was fantastic after a long day sightseeing.We were quoted 45 Euros fr a taxi from the airport so caught airport bus to Catalunya Square - Euro 3.20 and then Metro to hotel (10 underground trips for Euro 6.30). Need to use the Metro to get into town but they are every 5mins or so, cheap and it only takes about 15mins. Worth the journey out of town to stay in a quality hotel like this, rather than a same priced lower standard hotel in the centre.  
<Date>Jun 15, 2005
